The Provincial Representative Assembly has two missions: (1) The mission to the Chinese Kuomintang: since the Third National Congress in the 18th year (of the Republic of China), there have been many crises within the Party. Jiangsu is close to the Central Government and should bear a significant mission. Since the Third National Congress in the 18th year, there have been many crises within the Party. Jiangsu is close to the Central Government and should bear a significant mission. Comrades in all counties should unify their wills and work together for the progress of the Party. (2) The mission to the Party in this province: the reason why Party affairs in this province needed a second reorganization was entirely because there were small organizations within the Party, which caused disagreements and led to disputes, which is deeply regrettable. Now, the disputes in various counties have been eliminated and are on track, but since the Provincial Representative Assembly bears a significant mission for Party affairs in the entire province, it cannot harbor any selfish views or allow small organizations to disrupt Party affairs again. He was commissioned by the Central Government to attend the ceremony. At the same time, he was able to gather with representatives from various counties, which can also be said to be a gathering of all Party comrades in Jiangsu, a very rare opportunity. The chairman just reported that the mission of the Representative Assembly is very detailed. He wanted to say a few more words, which is the work of Party members. First, they must go to the countryside and go deep into the people to do work. Second, propaganda should not only make the people understand, but also pay attention to enlightening the people and making them have deep faith. The success of today's Provincial Representative Assembly is due to the guidance of the Party Committees of various provinces and the efforts of all comrades, a close organization, and continuous progress, which is why there is today's performance. The strength of the Party in the future will be easier to achieve good performance compared to today. However, completing the organization is only the first step. For example, a table, completing its organization is not the goal, but it is necessary to see how the strength it generates from its use is. The organization of the Party is the same. Now, the Party in the local area cannot be said to have no relationship with the people, but I think there is still a possibility of being more closely related. Photo of the Opening of the Jiangsu Provincial Representative Assembly 67

Wuhu Quick Dispatch 68

The Ministry of Interior and the Central Relief Committee, in order to establish standards for the future allocation of relief funds and issuance of disaster relief bonds, have sent special commissioners to investigate the disaster in seven provinces affected by floods, including Anhui and Hubei. Hong Hui, representing Anhui Province, will take a boat to Anqing tomorrow before coming to Wuhu to investigate the disaster in Southern Anhui.

Three thousand rickshaw pullers in Wuhu went on strike yesterday due to a conflict with boatmen. In addition to destroying more than 30 boats in various places, several people were injured. Nine rickshaw pullers were arrested by the Brigade Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau. That evening, the Public Security Bureau summoned representatives of the rickshaw pullers to persuade them, and they all resumed work this morning. However, the water level continued to rise by more than three inches today, making it even more difficult for rickshaws to operate in various places. More scaffolding is being built in various places, which has a greater impact on the rickshaw pullers' business.

A large group of bandits has been discovered on the border between Yingshan and Huoqiu counties in Anhui Province. In addition to the 53rd Division, which has been ordered to go and intercept them, Provincial Government Chairman Chen Tiaoyuan has also ordered troops from the 46th Division stationed in Liuan to send a regiment to suppress them.

Public Security Bureau Chief Zhao Jingshi convened a joint meeting of various agencies yesterday to conduct a grain registration. It was resolved that the Public Security Bureau, the County Government, and the County Chamber of Commerce would each send two people to form a grain registration office, which would be completed within three days. It was also decided to strictly prevent the export of grain under the pretext of military use.

A labor dispute broke out at the Swire Shipping Company's pier in Wuhu. Despite repeated arbitration, it has not been resolved. The British Consul in Nanjing sent Deputy Consul Gao Laicang to Wuhu yesterday to discuss the matter with County Magistrate Yu Yuying. Yu sent Niu Zigui to take over the engineering work, and it is hoped that the crisis will end. (August 14th)

松江 69

Three Bandit Leaders Including Zhang Tongsheng Executed by Firing Squad. Cao Pang, Commander of the Songhu Pacification Sub-district, and Fan Guozhong, former Captain of the First Water Police Team, captured lake bandit Tai Bao Ashu's subordinate, the pseudo-regimental commander, bandit leader Zhang Tongsheng (also known as Gaojiao Pai Si Quan), along with Miao Aye and Ruan Asan (also known as Dajiao Asan). After interrogation, they confessed to robbery and kidnapping without denial. Upon submitting the case to the Pacification Commissioner's Office, a true telegram approval was received. Today (the 15th) at noon, Zhang and the other two criminals were identified, bound, and escorted by a team to parade through the Ximen bustling market for a week, before being executed by firing squad at the Yuhuangge execution ground.

The case of the stolen goods at Tianmashan was solved. Yang Shijie, inspector of the Public Security Bureau, noticed two suspicious individuals in a small restaurant in the Cangqiao area this morning (the 15th). They had bundles on their backs and were eating. He stepped forward to question them and learned that one was Zhou Chunshan from Shandong, and the other was Tang Asi from Datuan. They admitted to stealing from a family whose name was unknown in the Tianmashan area. Upon searching the bundles, he discovered stolen goods such as silver ornaments and men's and women's clothing, totaling more than forty-three items. He immediately took them to the bureau for interrogation and detention pending investigation and handling.

Two More Robberies Occur Outside the South Gate. A robbery occurred in Changlou, outside the South Gate, last month, but the stolen goods and robbers have not been found. Unexpectedly, the home of a farmer named Zhou in the Twelfth and Thirteenth Tutu area was attacked by multiple bandits late on the fourteenth night. The victim was awakened from his sleep to find the robbers ransacking the room. They forced him to reveal the location of his hidden silver, but he refused, leading to him being beaten and injured. As a result, twenty yuan in silver dollars were robbed before the bandits escaped. At the same time, the home of a farmer named Wang in a neighboring village was also robbed, with forty-seven yuan in silver dollars being taken. The victims separately requested the Public Security Bureau and the County Court to arrest the bandits and recover the stolen goods this morning.

Change of Assistant Transportation Commissioner. Songjiang Assistant Transportation Commissioner Li Xianyang was transferred to be the Director of the West Bank Salt Transportation Bureau. The vacancy was filled by Lu Wenlan, recommended by the Ministry of Finance, who took office on the 15th. It is learned that the inauguration ceremony that day was quite grand, with guests including the chairman of the Salt Industry Association of the Five Districts of Jiangsu, various salt merchants, and representatives from various organizations.

Fengxian 70

River Works Case Prosecuted. The case of the Nanqiao Tang River Works, with the exception of the West Tang director Zhang Fengtai, who died of illness and the case was dismissed, the East Tang portion has been investigated by the Zhenjiang Court. The court has recognized the embezzlement; therefore, the case has been prosecuted by prosecutor Gu of that court, awaiting interrogation and judgment. However, the defendant Jiang Rongchu, and others (East Tang director) claimed that the errors were all due to negligence in accounting procedures. Yesterday, they specially hired a lawyer and submitted a petition to defend themselves.

Qingpu 71

Interception of Smuggled Opium Leads to the Drowning of a Patrol Officer. Fang Yi, the district chief of the Eleventh District, received a confidential report stating that there were suspicious boats, one large and one small, in the Xili area of Songjia Kan Town. The report requested a team be dispatched to inspect the boats. The district chief, upon receiving the report, together with the newly appointed patrol officer Zhang Xue, ordered four policemen to conduct an inspection. They found that the boat owner was Wang Changsheng and three others including Chen Qiaofu were on the boat. The small boat was a fishing boat, and the large boat had a cabin. Upon detailed interrogation, it was revealed that the boat was transporting 54 packages of opium belonging to Chen Liankui from Shanghai. The opium was hidden in the nearby residence of a Zhou family. The district chief and the patrol officer then led the original police team, guided by Chen and others, to investigate. Upon reaching the Zhou family's residence, suddenly

Page 14

three people swam away from the back door. The police team entered, leaving only an old woman. They thoroughly searched the residence and found a large number of illegal items. Just as they were about to continue their investigation, gunshots rang out. At that time, the district chief, the deputy district leader Jin Qiancheng, were surrounded by villagers. Patrol officer Zhang was shocked and fled. After the incident, he was nowhere to be found. The district chief then led the police to escort the two smugglers back to the district by boat with the contraband. The district chief first supervised the guards to escort the people and contraband to the county government for investigation. The next morning, the body of the patrol officer was found in the river behind the Zhou family's house. It is reported that the county government has appointed Shen Jinghua, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to supervise the inspection.

Kunshan 72

Opposition to Telephone Rate Increase. The telephones used by the Kunshan Telephone Company are mostly old, resulting in unclear pronunciation and difficult operators, causing users to complain. Previously, after a party-government meeting, a letter was sent to the county government, ordering the Construction Bureau to give the company a serious warning. However, no improvements have been seen to date. Instead, the company added a half-yuan monthly fee when collecting payments the day before yesterday. The users, arguing that the company had not notified them in advance and had unilaterally increased the fee, rose up in opposition. Chen Jiangang and others sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting the company to cancel the price increase and reorganize internally. Otherwise, they will unanimously refuse to pay the monthly fee.

Suzhou 73

Robbery and Injury in Meiyan Township. The home of Xu Yaofeng, a farmer in Meiyan Township, Wujiang County, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits on the night of the fourteenth. They wantonly ransacked the house. Before leaving, they fired a shot, hitting Xu Yaofeng's younger brother, Xu Yaoting, in the waist. He was severely injured and sent to Nanxun Hospital for treatment. His life is in grave danger.

Accomplice Arrested in the Case of Murdering One's Own Husband. Wang Caifa of Ducun, Hengjing Township, was murdered by his wife, Wang Jinshi, in collusion with her lover, Shi Lansheng. Shi Lansheng is still at large. Wang Jinshi has been sentenced to death by the local court. The accomplice Jin Wangshi fled to Suzhou and was working as a servant in the Li family in Xichengqiao. She was arrested yesterday (the 15th) and sent to the local court for interrogation.

Changshu 74

Electricity Users Temporarily Refuse to Pay Electricity Bills. The Electricity Users Association, due to the power plant outage for a month, suffered huge losses. On the eighth of this month, it convened all electricity users at the County Chamber of Commerce to elect five representatives to negotiate various matters with the company. The representatives have already submitted a written proposal to the manager of the power plant. The plant will now submit it to the board of directors to discuss and elect representatives to negotiate with the user representatives. All users are now following the association's proposal, resolutely refusing to pay electricity bills temporarily.

Ancient Sutra and Pagoda Map Discovered in the Ruined Pagoda of Meili. Meili Town, located sixteen miles east of the city in this county, is the leading town in the eastern countryside, exceptionally lively. There is a Dongta Temple in the east of the town. There was originally a Jusha Pagoda, which was about five to six zhang tall, built during the Song Dynasty. Later, due to years of disrepair, the temple fell into disuse, leaving only an open space of more than ten mu. The pagoda still stood alone in the middle, but it also showed signs of collapsing. Previously, people discovered several pages of the Diamond Sutra and a pagoda map, rolled up inside the bricks and tiles. The abbot of the temple, Yaozong, took custody of them. The district office (under the Meitang District) learned of the matter, put it on the meeting agenda, and sent someone to retrieve the items from the abbot to preserve the historical sites. However, it is said that the sutras and pagoda map were taken away by a Zhang, who hired someone to repair and bind them for safekeeping. Now, the district chief believes that the map and sutra were left from the Song Dynasty and are extremely rare treasures. He will negotiate with Zhang to hand them over.

Notorious Bandit Zheng Ming Has Been Sent to the County for Trial. The notorious bandit Zheng Ming is from Jiangbei. He grew up in Wangshi Town, Changshu, and followed his father, Zheng Yushan, in a life of banditry. He was arrested in Shanghai earlier this month. The detective team of this county's Public Security Bureau went to Shanghai to bring him back. On the twelfth, he was transferred from the Public Security Bureau to the county government. After a secret interrogation by Judge Chai, the bandit Zheng spoke generously, admitting that certain cases were done by him and his gang, while others were not, showing no fear. Knowing that he would not escape death, he asked the officials to write a letter to his mother before his execution by firing squad. He requested that his father's coffin also be transported back to Pu for burial. He had no other requests. He was then placed in heavy shackles and imprisoned, singing freely without any fear. It is said that Zheng Ming was extremely fierce since he was young. When he was eleven years old, he went to Hubei for some matter and hired a mule to travel to the station. The mule driver demanded payment, but Zheng had no money. He tricked the mule driver into going to the wilderness, where he stabbed the mule driver to death with a sharp knife. The villagers raised an alarm and gathered a crowd to surround and arrest Zheng, who was sentenced to six years in prison. Later, he was released during the general amnesty of the Beijing government in the tenth year. From this, one can see the extent of his cruelty.

Wuxi 75

Legal Officials Coerce Payment of Service Fees. Tianzhang Foreign Goods Store in Dangkou Town, the Eleventh District of the county, closed down in the spring of this year. Later, due to the difficulty in recovering debts owed by various households, a petition was specially submitted to the County Court for prosecution. After interrogation by President Yang of the court, it was revealed that there were as many as 172 households in Dangkou Town alone that owed money, and the total amount owed was only several hundred yuan. Recently, President Yang issued summons to the debtor households to come to the court for interrogation and recovery of the debts. Each summons charged a service fee of three yuan and five cents, totaling 524 yuan and six cents. The debtor households complained that some owed only one yuan or two or three yuan, and some had already paid off their debts but were still summoned to pay the service fee. They all complained to District Chief Yu Shangshu, requesting him to find a way to help. After District Chief Yu personally investigated, everyone said that the bailiffs of the court ordered them to raise and pay the service fee. If they did not comply, they would be sent to the Public Security Bureau for detention. As a result, public resentment was boiling. Dangkou and the court are only forty-five li apart, and the bailiffs can get more than 520 yuan in fees in one or two days, which is too much. The people cannot afford it. Yesterday, a letter was sent to President Yang, asking him to find a way to help and maintain the people's strength.

The First District Requests to Stabilize Rice Prices. Qian Zhongliang, the district chief of the First District, stated that this year's continuous rain has damaged the crops, causing rice prices to soar. Recently, one dan of white rice has risen to more than fourteen yuan. However, it is found that there is still a lot of rice stored in Wuxi. If hoarding can be prohibited and exports are stopped, rice prices will definitely be stabilized. Yesterday, he submitted a petition to the county government, requesting to reiterate the ban, strictly prevent hoarding, and convene rice merchants to suppress rice prices, and not allow them to raise prices and hoard, in order to maintain the people's food and stabilize people's hearts.

Vehicle Patrol Team Arrests a Bandit. Wang Wei, the captain of the County Police Brigade, ordered Huang Xiaoming, the leader of the vehicle patrol team, to lead patrol officer Zhang Guanghan, deputy squad leader Zhang Duoshan, and more than ten team members to patrol the countryside in vehicles the day before yesterday. While patrolling near Dongfeng, Xulei Bridge in the Third District (Yangming Township) outside the South Gate, they spotted three suspicious people sitting in a pavilion. They immediately stepped forward to question them. When the three people saw the police team, they ran away and fired their guns, fortunately without injuring anyone. Team leader Huang and others chased after them and arrested one person. The other two escaped. They also seized a rattan bag, a four-inch white Langlin pistol, five bullets, and clothing. They were all taken to the city for questioning. After interrogation, the arrested bandit claimed his name was Gu Gensheng, from Changzhou. He usually resides at his uncle's house in Yangshuyuan. The rest of his answers were vague. Yesterday, he was escorted to the brigade headquarters and transferred to the county government for handling.

Lake Water Backflows, Crops Are Hopeless. After the sunny days at the beginning of the month, the farmers tried to save the crops in the fields that had not been flooded, and it was expected to be effective. Until recently, the counties north of the Yangtze River have suffered floods, so the river water has not receded for days, and sometimes it has even increased. As of yesterday, the river water had receded by about eight inches. Because the river water did not recede, the effect of draining the fields was limited. The farmers were extremely anxious, so there was no certainty about the harvest.

Letter Requesting the Establishment of an Emergency Relief Association. The colleagues of the box office of the Gongyu Society at the railway station, in view of the major floods everywhere since the beginning of summer, where fields were washed away and cries of misery were everywhere, planned to gather all colleagues, sacrifice their image, and use all the funds raised from the sale of tickets for disaster relief. However, acting alone was of limited ability, and the funds raised were insufficient. Yesterday, a public letter was sent to the county party headquarters, requesting it to convene local organs and organizations to jointly organize and raise funds for emergency relief. The letter also requested that a location and date be designated to perform Peking opera for several days to raise funds for emergency relief.

Changzhou 76

Successive Robberies Occur at Dongzhi Bridge. The home of Wang Shunrong in Xinxin Village, near Dongzhi Bridge in the First District of Wuyi County, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits on the evening of the thirteenth. The bandits, each carrying guns, broke into the house and robbed it. While carrying the stolen goods, the bandits went to the Hongtai Teahouse in Diaozhuang Town. Seeing that people were gambling there, they broke in and robbed it again, taking all the silver dollars on the gambling table, amounting to seventy or eighty yuan.

Summary of Arrests of Bandits. The Detective Team of the Huyi County Government, in cooperation with detectives from the Second District of the Wuxi Water Police in Shanghai, arrested the notorious bandits Zhi Quanda and Peng Quangen from the Seventh District. Both were wanted criminals in major robbery and murder cases. They were brought back to Chang today (the 15th). In addition, the First District Shangyu Village Security Corps, etc., arrested the bandit Xu Aoqi in Huangtu Town, on the border of Wucheng, and the bandit Gu Zizhi in Shenjiatou. The two bandits were escorted to the city on the fourteenth, passing through Dabeimen. They encountered the notorious bandit Ni Hengda, who was also arrested. They were immediately sent to the Rural Clearing Bureau for interrogation.

Zhenjiang 77

Jindi Street and Lanes Are Inundated. Near the pier, Jiangnan streets and lanes are flooded because of river tides that have caused river water to reach the shore. The small pier, train station, Jinshan Intersection, and the Daguanlou area have turned into lakes. With water levels as high as knee-deep, residents living in water everyday are extremely miserable.

Mutual Transfer of Public Security Sub-Bureau Chiefs. The Provincial Public Security Bureau ordered Zhang Helu, the chief of the First Sub-Bureau, to be transferred to the Third Sub-Bureau. The vacancy was filled by the transfer of Shi Yun, the chief of the Seventh Sub-Bureau, and the ensuing vacancy was filled by the transfer of Xiao Hanjie, the chief of the Third Sub-Bureau.

Jintan 78

Establishment of the Disaster Relief Committee. This summer's excessive rainfall has caused severe damage in Tan County. On the twelfth of this month, the county government convened various organs and organizations to hold an inaugural meeting for the Jintan Branch of the Disaster Relief Committee. The meeting approved the revised charter and elected nine executive committee members to be responsible for handling the matter.

Nantong 79

Ministry of Transportation Commissions Survey of the Yangtze River Channel. The Ministry of Transportation commissioned Li Qiang to come to Nantong. On the fourteenth, he joined Dai Zhenmin, an engineer from the Construction Bureau, to survey the Yangtze River channel and the situation of collapsing banks to facilitate the planning and implementation of bank protection projects.

The Case of the Water Police Captain Being Stabbed Is Complex. Water Police Captain Xie Zezhi had a conflict with his former subordinate Yan Zheming. Yan stabbed Xie and fled to the court to appeal. He was chased and attacked by the water police in front of the court. Xie went to Shanghai more than a month ago and has not returned to Nantong. The court has scheduled an interrogation for the nineteenth. The County Lawyers Association appointed lawyer Zhang Shen to investigate the matter. Due to the complexity of the case, they sent a letter to the prosecutor's office, requesting a thorough investigation according to the law.

Change of Director of the Provincial Langshan Cotton Field. Xu Zhenzhou, the director of the Provincial Langshan Cotton Experiment Field, has passed away due to illness. Zhao Boji, the director of the Salt Reclamation Branch Field of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, has been temporarily appointed to replace him. Wang Zhihong has now been officially appointed as the director.

Investigation and Prohibition of Coastal Fishermen Purchasing Bandit Protection Passes. The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Industry stated that many coastal fishermen have recently been purchasing counterfeit protection passes from sea bandits. In addition to sending warships to patrol the sea and protect fishermen, the bureau has ordered the county to investigate and prohibit the purchase of these passes to cut off the bandits' financial support.

Yangzhou 80

The River Water in Yangzhou Suddenly Rose by About a Foot. Although the Grand Canal dike is under tension, the Zhaoguan Dam will not be opened for the time being. Various parties in the province and government advocate protecting the dike. The details were reported earlier. It is now learned that the people upstream and downstream have a rumor that the Zhaoguan Dam will be opened on a certain day. Therefore, thousands of people gathered to protect the dike. On the thirteenth and fourteenth nights, many people rushed to the dike, and the lights were as bright as day. Jiangdu upstream rose two inches on the fourteenth, still recovering the water level of two feet and four inches. Downstream, when the afternoon tide arrived, the Grand Canal outside Dongguan, Quekou, Chaoguan, Fuyun, and Xunningmen, etc., around the city, suddenly rose by about a foot, and the water flooded into the city more deeply. On the thirteenth, the boats traveling between Yangzhou and Zhenjiang could go straight through the Baota Gate south of the city without detouring the three bends because of the high water level. On the afternoon of the fourteenth, the water in Slender West Lake suddenly became turbid, from east to west. Those who wanted to go to Tianningmen by small boat north of the city were blocked by the turbidity. The sidewalk on Lower Buying and Selling Street was submerged past the knees. According to a message from the Construction Bureau on the fourteenth, the Zixi dikes of Shaobo (about eight li) have already been built, but the dikes will lose effect again due to the high water level. Xu Mingdi, the technology section chief of the Construction Bureau stationed in the town, and section member Wang Ruisheng, added three feet of zixi dikes to the area from the Nandawang Temple to the Beiban Factory, which will be completed soon. A special report was submitted to the bureau and the county, requesting to send personnel to inspect and accept the dikes on the sixteenth. Chen County Chief and Zhang Zuan, the director of the Construction Bureau, personally went to Yangzi Bridge to investigate both banks. Because that place is the main road to the Yangtze River, the banks are in a very critical situation. It is planned to carry out rescue work.

Gaoyou 81

The Northern Spur of the Nanguan Dam Cracked. The Nanguan Dam in this county, which leads to the sea, was secretly opened on the night of the fourth. The Water Conservancy Bureau has been employing workers to repair the dam day and night because the northern spur of the dam has been damaged for a long time. Unexpectedly, at about 5:00 AM this morning (the 11th), the northern spur suddenly cracked, which is extremely dangerous. A gong was immediately struck to signal for rescue. The danger has not been removed. If the dam spur collapses, the Grand Canal dike north of the dam will also collapse, and the city of Gaoyou and the four counties below will become a lake.

Rugao 82

Two Regiments Go to Sea to Suppress Sea Bandits. The Fengli City Fishermen's Association and the Security Corps set off (on the afternoon of the 11th) to go to sea to suppress the sea bandits. At 9:00 AM the next morning, in the Shayuwa area, they approached the bandits' boat and immediately surrounded and attacked it. Both sides bombed each other for thirty minutes. The bandits could not hold out and fled east. In this battle, several bandits were killed, four fishing boats were recaptured, and twelve hostages were rescued.

The Fengli District Chief Is Dismissed. Zhong Guang, the Fengli District Chief, has now been dismissed by the county magistrate. The vacancy has been temporarily filled by assistant Zhang Tang.

Hangzhou 83

Young Man Commits Suicide by Poisoning Due to an Affair. On the afternoon of the 14th of this month, at 2:00 PM, a young man from Shanghai, Du Hongchun, 26 years old and from Haining, booked room 80 at the Hangzhou Hotel on Hubin Road. He immediately called the tea boy to get a pen and write two letters. He went out once at 5:00 PM and went to Pishi Lane after dinner. He returned to the hotel at 9:30 PM, closed the door, and went to bed. At 2:00 AM today (the 15th), the tea boy passed by the door and saw that the guest had not gotten up. He pushed the door open and entered, seeing that the guest's face was pale and his mind was confused. On the table, there was an empty bottle of sleeping pills and a small empty box of opium. Knowing that he had taken poison, he urgently called the police station to send police to Hangzhou Hospital for treatment. After twenty emergency injections, there was still no improvement by 4:00 PM in the afternoon. His life was feared to be difficult to save. One of the suicide notes requested the court to waive the autopsy. It stated that he worked for the telephone bureau in Shanghai and other places. Two years ago, he returned to his hometown and met a young woman. Their love was very good. This year, they were discovered by a neighbor and suffered a major shock. He bought the sleeping pills and opium in Shanghai. He heard that the woman was in Hangzhou, so he could not bear to leave her and came here to commit suicide.

The Provincial Committee Secretly Investigates Rice Smuggling. After merchants from other provinces purchased rice in large quantities in Xiashi, Pinghu, and other places in Zhejiang Province, the price of rice in Hangzhou soared by nearly two yuan in three days. After the province ordered a ban on transportation, the price dropped slightly. From yesterday, the price of rice rose again and increased further. It will increase by seven or eight yuan soon. It is heard that the provincial government has secretly sent special commissioners to Pinghu, Jiashan, Xitang, and other places to secretly investigate smuggling. It has also telegraphed the water police to earnestly supervise and detain any rice being transported and report it to the provincial government for handling.

Establishment of an Association to Manage Public Debt. The Zhejiang Provincial Government has established a fund management committee to manage the 8 million yuan in public debt issued to clear old debts. Twenty gentry and merchants were hired as management committee members. The committee was established yesterday at a meeting in the Finance Department. Wang Xiangquan, Zhang Xuren, Xu Xinlu, and three others were elected as executive committee members.

Yuhang 84

The People of the Entire County Oppose Increased Taxes. The surcharges and taxes on Yuhang's land tax are almost twice the amount of the regular tax. The people have suffered from consecutive years of disasters and famines and are impoverished. In May of this year, the education community took advantage of the expiration of the three-year limit for the grain accumulation fund and continued to collect funds for the righteous education grain accumulation. The grain accumulation was collected at a rate of four cents of ocean per mu of land, which was still not satisfactory. Therefore, the land and mountains were included as a whole and collected at a rate of five cents of ocean per mu. The righteous education received four cents, and the grain accumulation received one cent. The education director Cheng Feng and others submitted a request to the county government for approval and transfer. County Magistrate Feng Shifan only invited the education community and held a meeting at the government office. He then used the name of approval by the various legal groups to submit the request to the higher authorities for approval. After the procedures were completed, the collection was announced. Upon hearing this, the people of the entire county were shocked. The sixty villages and eighty-six communities in the six districts of the county, the county farmers' association, and the people all submitted requests to the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the three ministries of finance, civil affairs, and education, requesting the original plan be withdrawn. The provincial government approved the request and ordered the three ministries to discuss and respond to it. The people waited for a month but there was no indication. They then elected representatives to go to the province to petition. On the morning of the fourteenth, the representatives went to the provincial government to request an audience. Secretary Lou Jin Jian received them. The representatives presented the facts that County Magistrate Feng and others had deceived their superiors and forged public opinion. Secretary Lou recognized that the representatives' request was justified and agreed to submit it to the Provincial Government Committee for reconsideration. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Xiaoshan 85

Rice Prices Soar, the Common People Cry Out in Distress. Xiaoshan has always relied on external supplies of rice. Recently, because the new goods have not arrived and the old goods have been used because of the floods in various places, the price of rice has risen sharply. In the past week, the price per dan in Xiaoshan City has risen to more than one yuan. As of yesterday, the price had increased by six jiao per grade. The price of three coarse white late rice was 12.6 yuan, the price of secondary goods was 12.4 yuan, and the starting price was 9.8 yuan. Ordinary people were complaining because they could not afford to buy the rice.

A Gale Blows Down a Wall, Crushing Two Children to Death. The young son of Wu Jifa, a farmer in Houwu, outside the East Gate, and a young daughter of the Cai family next door disappeared while playing outside on the afternoon of the ninth. The family searched everywhere without success and suspected that they had been abducted. Unexpectedly, a fierce wind blew down the wall behind Wu's house that day. The two children were crushed to death.

Hangzhou Newspaper Studies Summer School Closing Ceremony 88

The Hangzhou branch of the China Newspaper Studies Society held a summer newspaper studies training course, and successively invited Pan Gongbi, Pan Gongzhan, Guo Butao, Fan Zhongyun, Huang Tianpeng, Zhou Shang, Zhu Shaoping, Li Xueyong, Xu Paoting, Huang Jiping, Xu Xin and others from Shanghai to give lectures. After the examination, 51 people passed and 19 people were allowed to retake the exam. The closing ceremony was held on August 13, presided over by Ge Gongzhen, with speeches by Zhang Daofan, Director of the Education Department, and Sun Weikui, Zhang Zhengfan, and Xiang Shiyuan. The student representative, Jing Guanzhi, gave a thank-you speech, followed by a group photo and dismissal.

In addition, the newspaper exhibition held by the society at the same time, using the museum as the venue, displayed thousands of types of newspapers and magazines. The items were divided into four major rooms, with the most exhibits coming from Xiang Shiyuan and Zhong Yunyu, which were valuable and highly praised by society, marking an unprecedented event in China. It also closed on the 15th.

Local News

Today's Opening of the National 89

National Language Discussion Conference 90

Opening ceremony held at the Imperial Palace Theater in the morning

General meeting of members held at Gongdelin in the afternoon

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association convened the National Mandarin Education Discussion Conference. The opening ceremony will be held at 8:30 this morning at the Imperial Palace Grand Theater on Xizang Road, Shanghai. The following are the latest news:

I. Representatives Attending 91

Representatives attending, from the government side, included representatives from the Education Departments of Fujian, Hubei, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Anhui, Shandong, and Zhejiang, representatives from the Education Bureaus of Shanghai and Nanjing, and representatives from the Shantou, Guangdong and Rucheng, Hunan branches. On the membership side, there were 110 people from Sichuan, Guangdong, Guangxi, Fujian, Hunan, Hubei, Zhejiang, Shandong, Anhui, and other places.

II. Venue Arrangement 92

The conference venue was set up in the newly opened Imperial Palace Small Theater. The national flag and the banner "National Mandarin Education Discussion Conference" were hung at the entrance. In addition to Chinese characters, the characters on the banner also included phonetic symbols and Mandarin Romanization. In the center of the stage hung the portrait of the Premier, the national flag, and the banner for the 20th Anniversary Member Congress. On the left hung the four characters "National Language Unification" and the opening order banner. On the right hung the four characters "Language and Writing Consistency" and the conference schedule banner. A cloth banner with the words "National Mandarin Education Discussion Conference" hung at the entrance.

III. First Day's Schedule 93

A preparatory meeting was held at 8:30 a.m. on August 16, with Lu Yiyan appointed as the temporary chairman by the conference office. The agenda included (1) reporting on the purpose of the preparatory meeting, (2) electing the presidium, (3) electing the conference secretary, and (4) taking photos. The opening ceremony of the National Mandarin Education Discussion Conference and the 20th Anniversary Member Congress was held at 9:00 a.m. (see yesterday's newspaper for the opening order). At 12:00 noon, the National Mandarin Education Promotion Association held a welcome reception at Gongdelin on Park Road. The 20th Anniversary Member Congress was held at 2:00 p.m., and a garden party was held at Chen's Garden on Seymour Road from 4:30 p.m.

V. Member Congress 94

The 20th Anniversary Member Congress is scheduled to be held at Gongdelin at 2:00 p.m. today. The order is as follows: (1) Salute to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of the Premier, (2) Read the Premier's will respectfully, (3) Silent tribute, (4) Opening remarks, (5) Discussion of proposals, (6) Elections, (7) Adjournment.

VI. Conference Proposals 95

There were eighteen proposals for the 20th Anniversary Member Congress, divided into four categories:

Regarding organization: 1. Request the directors of this association to raise funds for the association to facilitate development (Executive Committee of this association). 2. Request the Board of Directors of this association to submit a request to the Nanjing Municipal Government for the allocation of public land to build the headquarters of the association (Executive Committee of this association). 3. Request this association to broadly solicit Mandarin comrades across the country to promote Mandarin education (Peng Jianong). 4. Mandarin Education Promotion Associations should be established in provinces, cities, and counties to facilitate promotion (proposed by Fujian Education).

Regarding training: 5. Request this association to open a Mandarin teacher training institute to cultivate Mandarin talents (Yuan Wen). 6. Request this association to open a Mandarin correspondence course to facilitate Mandarin study by comrades in various local areas (Wu Yue). 7. Request this association to attach a Mandarin model school to continue operations (Hu Shouren). 8. Request this association to run a long-term Mandarin specialty school for a period of one year to cultivate Mandarin talents and promote Mandarin education (Zhao Yunzhi).

Regarding promotion: 9. Send a letter to chambers of commerce in provinces, cities, and counties across the country, requesting them to inform shops to add Mandarin Romanization to shop signs or advertising text (Li Weiyue). 10. Send a letter to chambers of commerce in provinces, cities, and counties across the country, requesting them to inform shops to add Mandarin phonetic symbols to shop signs or advertising text (Pei Weisen). 11. Send a circular to hometown associations and other organizations in various cities across the country, urging them to pay attention to the Mandarin education of children from their hometowns (Li Weiyue). 12. Send a letter to libraries across the country, requesting them to collect more Mandarin and standard pronunciation books and find ways to circulate them (Li Weiyue). 13. Send a letter to newspapers across the country, requesting them to add phonetic symbols and Mandarin Romanization to the newspaper titles (Peng Jianong). 14. Send a letter to national mass education centers, requesting them to display Mandarin books (Lu Yiyan).

Regarding publicity: 15. Request the publicity department of this association to broadcast Mandarin speeches related to Mandarin publicity on the radio station every Saturday (Zhang Shicheng). 17. Request this association to publish a Mandarin phonetic symbol weekly (Zhu Mianxian). 18. Request this association to organize a publicity team to go to the Nanyang area in July to promote Mandarin phonetic symbols and Mandarin Romanization (Zhu Mianxian).

Jinan University to Administer Entrance Exams for Feng Yong University 98

The number of applicants was not high on the 17th and 18th

National Jinan University's enrollment of new students this year has been going very well for the past three days. The school will also be administering entrance exams for Feng Yong University of Shenyang starting tomorrow. Feng University stands tall on the frontier, meticulously pursuing academics, and is renowned both in the north and south. Students who graduate from the school also have the hope of being sent abroad for further studies. The school also offers preferential treatment such as free tuition, half tuition, and tuition reductions. It is reported that the number of applicants in Shanghai is not high. Aspiring young people can go and try their luck. The middle school department is also enrolling students at the same time.

"World Magazine" Releases 10th Anniversary Special Edition 99

The "World Magazine," published by the Shanghai World Book Company, is rich in content and published on schedule, and has long been recognized by people across the country. Its circulation is unprecedented in the domestic magazine industry, reaching more than 40,000 copies for domestic and foreign subscribers alone, not including retail sales. Recently, in commemoration of the book company's 10th anniversary, a special "Tenth Anniversary" issue was published, written by experts from home and abroad. The content includes China's politics in the past ten years, China and the League of Nations in the past ten years, China's diplomacy in the past ten years, China's municipal administration in the past ten years, China's economy in the past ten years, China's international trade in the past ten years, China's laws in the past ten years, China's cooperative movement in the past ten years, China's education in the past ten years, China's engineering education in the past ten years, China's literature in the past ten years, China's drama in the past ten years, the Mandarin movement in the past ten years, the world literary scene in the past ten years, Esperanto in the past ten years, and many other topics. The magnificent volume, with its 300,000 words, is truly a spectacle in the magazine world. Since its publication, several thousand copies have been sold in less than a week. It is reported that pre-orders for volumes three and four will begin today at the Shanghai headquarters and branch offices in various provinces and cities. It is also reported that the content of the magazine will be further enriched from volume three onwards in order to meet the wishes of readers.

Sports

Rotary Cup War Opens

Canada Takes Advantage, England and Japan Tie 100

Canada wins two singles against the United States

England and Japan each win one singles

Today at 4:30 PM | England-Japan Doubles Group | Canada-United States Singles Group

The second Shanghai Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament began yesterday afternoon at 3:30 p.m. at the Central Tennis Courts. The athletes from the United States, Canada, England, and Japan entered the arena with great enthusiasm, showing off their skills and striving for glory. As a result, Canada won both singles matches against the United States, and England and Japan each won one singles match. Starting at 4:30 p.m. today, an England-Japan doubles group and a United States-Canada singles group will be held at the same venue. In addition, all the tennis balls used in this tournament were donated by Dunlop, totaling fifteen dozen.

Canada Wins Both Singles

| American Players Lack Resistance | 101

Devoe Defeats Opponent with Ease 102

Devoe (Canada) (6|2 6|4 6|1) Smith (USA)

Devoe came from Canada this year and is one of their famous players. He has long arms, a comfortable grip, and is good at doubles and singles. Yesterday, he met Smith, and struck out easily, breaking the enemy's line with ease. The first set was 6-2, and the victory and defeat passed in a flash. In the second set, Smith's offense and defense improved, and he showed some resistance, but he could not hold on for long. After 4-4, he saw a downward trend again and soon lost again with 4-6. In the third set, Devoe's long arms waved left and right, and he was invincible. Smith lost all his fighting power and almost didn't know what to do. He won back a game, avoiding being blanked, which was a great blessing in misfortune. As a result, Devoe won a big victory with 6-1.

Canada-United States First Singles (Zhao Fang Photography) (Left) Devoe from Canada (Right) Smith from the United States 103

Ritt's Divine Power Finally Leads to Victory 104

Ritt (Canada) (3|6 6|4 2|6 6|3 6|2) Squires (USA)

Of the four singles matches on the day, the most intense was Ritt vs. Squires. The number of wins and losses for both players was fiercely contested in every point, every game, and every set. However, Ritt's final victory in the fifth set relied on his strong divine power. Initially, Squires won the first set 6-3. Then Ritt fought back and won the second set 6-4. Squires then won the third set 6-2, taking the lead. Ritt then won the fourth set 6-3, creating a tie. After four sets, Squires' face was pale, and his arm strength was greatly reduced. Ritt took advantage of the momentum and advanced rapidly, dominating the situation. In comparison, the difference between the two became apparent. Before long, Ritt won the fifth set 6-2.

Devoe vs. Squires Today 106

England and Japan Split the Spoils

| Each Wins One Singles | 107

Hyotare Effort to Break Through Three Barriers 108

Hyotare (Japan) (6|3 1|6 6|2) Tuck (England)

Hyotare is worthy of being a famous singles player, breaking through three barriers in a row and defeating Tuck, a veteran of England. In the first set, the two closely followed each other, resisting each other. Hyotare was good at using arm strength and succeeded in everything he wanted. Tuck relied on his experience and advanced whenever he had the chance. After 2-2, Hyotare specialized in attacking the opponent's weaknesses, and Tuck could not correct them, losing two games in a row. It seemed that there was a turning point under the hard counterattack, but unexpectedly the net shot lost its balance, either committing suicide in front of the net or hitting wildly outside the shallow area. With a long sigh, he failed with 3-6. In the second set, Hyotare's victory was due to his superb artistry, but Tuck's repeated suicides and inaccurate angles also indirectly contributed to his victory. As a result, 6-1. In the third set, Tuck seemed to feel powerless, and Hyotare's smashes were fierce, like a hurricane, making people shudder. He won five games in a row. Tuck fought like a trapped beast, showing all his skills as much as possible, winning back two games, and making some progress. Hyotare was deeply afraid of losing his success and worked hard, finally winning again with 6-2.

Veteran Wheat's Power Remains 110

Wheat (England) (6|3 6|1 6|4) Machida (Japan)

Veteran Wheat has been a hero at sea for many years. When his reputation was at its peak, today's good players were probably still learning to hold the racket and serve the ball. Time flies, but Wheat, although old, is still serving his motherland. He played yesterday, and his power remained. The agile and lively Machida ran under his control, relying on others' breath, and sighed that he was inferior. In the first set, each used the serve to gain momentum alternately. Until each had two, Machida's weaknesses were fully revealed. The old general seized the opportunity to attack, and he didn't miss one in a hundred. He turned around and won with 6-3. In the second set, Machida was too depressed. Except for winning in the fifth game, he failed in one game after another, and finally lost badly with 1-6. In the middle of the third set, Wheat showed signs of fatigue. Machida took advantage of this to go straight up, holding an advantage of 4-2. How could the old general Wheat be willing to fall behind? His spirit was refreshed, and his muscle strength was restored. He won four games in a row, turning defeat into victory, creating a result of 6-4.

Local News

China Merchants Bureau Jinliyuan Wharf Case 115

Resolved by Signing Yesterday 116

The Bureau Prepared to Pay 275,000 Taels to Purchase

Secretary Bao Published Detailed Account of the Incident Yesterday

Huadong News Agency reports: The case of the dispute between the China Merchants Bureau and the French Catholic Church's Sande Hall over the foundation of Jinliyuan Wharf No. 69 has gone through procedures such as lawsuits, mediation, adjudication, and negotiations for a year and a half. The opinions of the two parties differed, making it difficult to resolve. It was not until recently, when Commissioner Guo of the Bureau continued to handle the matter, that they gradually approached an agreement. Yesterday morning, they officially signed a resolution. Sande Hall was willing to sell the land to the Bureau for 275,000 taels, and the Bureau immediately paid the full amount and completed the handover. The eighteen-month-long case has been resolved at once, which is noteworthy.

Mr. Bao Gongfan, Secretary of the China Merchants Bureau, yesterday told a reporter from the Huadong News Agency about the beginning and end of the case. The content of the dispute was that both sides had foundations, both rented by the China Merchants Bureau. One side built a warehouse to store goods, and the other was the Jinliyuan Wharf. The section in the middle, where Warehouse No. 21 was built, was of great importance to the entire wharf. Therefore, when the issue of tax increases arose during the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, the Minister of Beiyang and the Shanghai Daotai made every effort to insist on negotiations. Although they were ultimately forced to yield after more than eight years, and land rights were seized, they were fortunately able to secure the condition that it would not hinder the Bureau's shipping operations, so the Bureau was able to continue renting the land. Unexpectedly, in October of the eighteenth year, the China Merchants Bureau exceeded the deadline for paying the winter rent by four days. Although the Bureau later paid the amount with interest calculated on a daily basis, Sande Hall announced the termination of the lease contract on this basis, and in December of that year, filed a lawsuit in the French Concession's Joint Court to terminate the contract. On January 7 of the nineteenth year, the judgment was in favor of the termination of the contract. The Bureau was forced to apply for a retrial. In May, the retrial also failed. However, the valuation of the buildings on the ground was allowed to be determined by appraisers appointed by both parties. The two lawsuits thus resulted in losses. In August, when Cai Pei, Director of the Navigation Affairs Department of the Ministry of Communications, concurrently served as the General Manager of the Bureau, in view of the urgency of the case, realized that if it was not resolved, the adjudication period would expire in an instant, and the Joint Court would inevitably execute the judgment. He began to adopt mediation methods, with the Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Shanghai and the French Consul-General acting as mediators. One side tried to postpone the execution period, while negotiating back and forth. The newly appointed Commissioner Li Zhonggong took over the matter in September and continued to mediate according to the procedure. After several negotiations, the church side agreed to sell the wharf portion of the land to the Bureau for 390,000 taels. However, because the numbers were too far apart, it was impossible to compromise. The arbitrators appointed by both parties also had different views, and no results could be obtained. After such twists and turns, the matter was delayed for several months, and there was still no concrete solution until the spring of this year. Since Commissioner Guo took office, he has directly met and negotiated with Father Xiaqi of Sande Hall. Father Xiaqi initially held out for a high price and refused to sell easily. Later, after Guo's multiple negotiations, Father Xiaqi was finally able to comply, and the land was sold for a price of 275,000 taels. The Bureau has paid the money and formally completed the handover. The year-long case has been resolved at once, allowing land rights that had been lost to foreigners for decades to be returned to their original owner. This is also a cause for celebration.

Yu Fengzhi Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 117

Staying at the Jianghaiguan Supervisory Office

Returning to Peiping after the Funeral of Mother Song

Ms. Yu Fengzhi, wife of Deputy Commander Zhang, arrived in Shanghai from Peiping on behalf of Deputy Commander Zhang to pay respects to the funeral of Mother Song, Mrs. Ni. She arrived by train at 4:50 p.m. yesterday. Those who came with her included Shen Nengyi, Director of the Printing Bureau of the Ministry of Finance of Peiping, Mr. and Mrs. Xu Tonghai, Advisor to the Peiping Municipal Government, and more than a dozen adjutants, bodyguards, and servants. The Railway Bureau specially prepared a flower car, attached to the special express train, which departed from Beijing at 10:00 a.m. yesterday and arrived at the North Station on time without delay. The station area and the platform were filled with military police with guns and live ammunition, and security was extremely tight. Traffic was temporarily cut off when the train entered the station. The military band of the Garrison Command and the Public Security Bureau went to the station to play music. After getting off the train, Ms. Yu Fengzhi, accompanied by Mrs. Mayor Zhang, walked out of the platform under strict protection and took the No. 9228 car prepared by the Municipal Government and went straight to the inner courtyard of the Jianghaiguan Supervisory Office on Xinzha Road to rest. This was specially prepared by the Song residence's funeral arrangement office in advance, and the food and lodging were more comfortable. Ms. Yu stayed there yesterday. As for the staff, they stayed at the Cangzhou Hotel, where the funeral arrangement office also set aside ten rooms to provide accommodation. According to sources close to Ms. Yu, she came here specifically to pay respects to the funeral, and will return to Peiping after the funeral of Mrs. Song. When Ms. Yu got off the train yesterday, she wore a dark blue floral gauze cheongsam, lightly applied makeup, and her face was radiant. When she walked out of the platform, she chatted and laughed with Mrs. Mayor Zhang along the way, and nodded to the welcomers to express her gratitude. After arriving at the Jianghaiguan Supervisory Office, Ms. Yu rested for a while and went to the Song residence on Seymour Road to meet Mrs. Chiang Song Meiling and others, and paid respects to Mother Song's coffin as required. She left after talking for half an hour.

Memorial Portrait of Mother Song, Mrs. Ni 121

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Requests

Opinions on Revising the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement 122

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to various trade guilds, stating: "We are writing to inform you that on the 13th of this month, we received a letter from the Committee for Studying the Sino-Japanese Agreed Tariff Rates. It stated that the tariff rates stipulated in the Sino-Japanese Reciprocal Tariff Agreement are still significantly disparate and that the agreement is about to expire and should be revised urgently. The National Products Preservation Association and other organizations convened a joint meeting of various groups and organized the Committee for Studying the Sino-Japanese Agreed Tariff Rates, which held its inaugural meeting on August 5th. At the first committee meeting, it was decided to request the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce to send a circular to various trade guilds to solicit their opinions on the revisions that should be made to the Sino-Japanese Agreed Tariff Rates. This would allow for research and review before submitting them to the Ministry for adoption. Upon investigation, this Sino-Japanese reciprocal tariff agreement has been in effect since May 16, 1930. The agreement period is divided into two types. One is a one-year term, which refers to Japanese general merchandise such as fragrant mushrooms, enameled washbasins, enameled ironware, buttons, cloth umbrellas, mirrors, boots, shoes, clocks, watches, hats, medicines, automatic thermostats, suitcases, briefcases, satchels, business card cases, various travel suitcases and boxes, vehicles, and bicycles. The validity of this agreement expired on May 16, 1931. Our business community did not request the government to pay attention to the revision, which was a missed opportunity. The other type, including cotton goods, fish, seafood, etc., has a three-year term and can only be revised on May 16, 1933. The "expiration is imminent, urgently needs to be revised" mentioned by the research committee refers to this three-year term. In summary, regarding the reciprocal items between the two countries, Japan gains 63 types, including 33 types of cotton products, 12 types of seafood, and 17 types of wheat flour and sundries, while China only gains 3 types: summer cloth, silk fabrics, and handmade embroidery. In terms of the reciprocal tariff rates, the majority of China's items maintain the import tariff rates of 1929, and only a few can increase by 2.5%. Therefore, the impact of the so-called new tax (i.e., the tariff rate implemented from January 1, 1931) on Japan is not significant. On the other hand, Japan does not reduce the tariff rates on China's imported summer cloth and embroidery. The tariff on silk fabrics is reduced from 100% to 70%, but its effectiveness is also very minor. Therefore, it is called reciprocal in name, but in reality, it is one-sided. This time, when the committee collects opinions, various industries should pay attention to the following two matters: (1) They must select products or semi-finished products that have a history of sales or potential for sales in Japan. As for the raw materials needed by Japan, the tax is inherently light for the sake of protecting Japanese industries, so there is no need to propose them on our own. (2) For Japanese products that have the potential to severely compete with China's emerging industries, a detailed investigation should be conducted on the relationship between the benefits and harms of both parties. The reciprocal tariff rates should be abolished, or like Japan's treatment of our silk fabrics, a maximum tariff rate should be set, and then slightly reduced. The above-mentioned situation is to prevent various industries from not being fully aware of the details and interests of the Sino-Japanese reciprocal agreement. Therefore, a brief summary is provided for reference during research. If there are any brilliant ideas, please send them to the association for forwarding."

Municipal Government

Exempting Poor Households from House Tax 124

Partial Exemption for Tenants from This Autumn

The municipal government levies house tax. For those whose monthly rent is less than one yuan or quarterly rent is less than three jiao, they are mostly poor laborers with insufficient income to support their families. The Finance Bureau was previously instructed to grant exemptions to show compassion. Recently, the municipal government, in order to show extra compassion for poor households, will, starting from this autumn, exempt the tenant's portion of the house tax for households in the city whose rent is less than three yuan per month or whose quarterly rent is less than nine jiao, except for the owner's portion, which will be collected according to regulations. However, the outstanding taxes from previous quarters will still be urged by the Finance Bureau to collect in a harmonious manner to conclude the matter.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce: The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a declaration yesterday regarding the kidnapping of people by Japanese soldiers in the Huangpu River. The most prominent examples are the Jinan May 30th Incident and the recent Wanbaoshan Incident. According to international practice, such actions can only be applied to conquered or occupied territories. This shows that the Japanese have long ceased to recognize China as an independent and autonomous country. Otherwise, if the two countries have diplomatic officials, why not use diplomatic procedures to resolve matters and instead resort to force and free action? This shows that Japan's policy towards China has not changed and there is no sincerity in repenting. From this, we can draw two conclusions: (1) Our citizens should have a clearer understanding of Japan and further strengthen their spirit of perseverance. (2) It proves that the Japanese have recognized that our people's movement has an irresistible force. Therefore, they have resorted to this desperate and perverse means. In this situation, we can only continue to strive peacefully to achieve the final victory. This is our declaration."

Exchanging Opinions on Anti-Japanese and Overseas Chinese Aid

Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Ye Huijun, Wang Yansong, Yuan Ludeng, and Xu Jilu hosted a public banquet for leaders of various industries at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce the night before last. Yu Qiaqing is a veteran of the business community and was invited to express his views first. Yu said that boycotting Japanese goods must be sustained and not be… timely. Only by having goods to boycott can we control others. For example, fine yarn, etc., our country does not yet have this product and cannot but purchase it from them. Therefore, for raw material necessities, we can only endure the pain and purchase them for the time being. On the one hand, we collect national salvation funds to prepare factories for manufacturing raw materials. Only considering the present and not the future is not a permanent solution. In short, when boycotting Japanese goods, we must also consider the livelihood of domestic workers. Matters that cause international negotiations should be avoided. Various industries should encourage each other to inspire their conscience and not sell Japanese goods. Because our country's tariffs are not completely autonomous, preventing foreign goods is very difficult. Today, we invite you to express your opinions so that we can exchange them and agree on appropriate methods. The detained goods should be returned, because the Chinese people have already invested in these goods, and prolonged detention has nothing to do with the Japanese, etc. Qiu Liangyu detailed the painstaking efforts of the Japanese to instigate the Koreans to排華. Please submit anti-Japanese opinions in writing to the Chamber of Commerce. The methods for assisting overseas Chinese will be discussed first tonight. Chen Liangyu stated that the previous boycotts of Japanese goods were not thorough. Now, fathers should urge their sons, and brothers should encourage their brothers. This time, we must not repeat the mistakes of the five-minute heat. Lu Qisheng said that the people's spontaneous boycott will not cause international negotiations. Wang Yansong, Ye Jiaxing, and others then expressed their opinions. As a result, it was agreed that the business community would unanimously boycott Japanese goods spontaneously. All inspection and investigation work will be handled by each industry to avoid harassment.

The United States Plans to Transport Wheat to China for Disaster Relief 132

The Continental Daily reports that yesterday (14th) it was rumored in this city that the Chinese flood disaster relief authorities are in contact with responsible American merchants to transport 30 million bushels of wheat from the United States to China to provide food for the disaster areas. This wheat will be sold on credit to the Chinese government, with a long repayment period. Currently, the United States is suffering from a wheat surplus and is urgently seeking sales channels. However, various provinces in China are experiencing an unprecedented flood disaster. Not only are the victims currently without food and clothing, but also most of the national autumn harvest has been destroyed. The future is long. If there is no suitable relief method, it is feared that it will lead to chaos. Therefore, if this can become a reality, both China and the United States will benefit.

"Fa Shang New Hotel" 134

Two Travelers Murdered in Revenge 135

Thugs Monitor the Hotel Owner

Saying There is No Need to Announce the Revenge

Gunshots Crack Like Machine Guns

Two Travelers Die of Serious Injuries

At the "Fa Shang New Hotel" on West Xinqiao Street in the French Concession, at around 7:30 last night, a revenge murder case occurred involving gunshots. At the time, two travelers were shot dead by thugs, and two others were seriously injured. The perpetrators fled without a trace. The details are as follows:

Two Men Check into a Room: The "Fa Shang Hotel" is located at No. 113 West Xinqiao Street in the French Concession. Yesterday afternoon at around 2 pm, two men came to check into a room. The waiter led them to Room No. 2 on the ground floor. One guest was wearing white pants and shirt, and the other was wearing yellow shorts, a white collared shirt, and a Western-style undershirt. They were about 36 or 37 years old. They wrote the name "Wang Xiji" in the register. Both were bare-handed, without luggage, and behaved rudely. After sitting in the room for a few minutes, they went out together, paying a room fee of one silver dollar.

Four Thugs Suddenly Break In: At around 7:15 in the evening, the two travelers calling themselves "Wang Xiji" returned from outside with two other men, one wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, and the other wearing white shorts. Both were around 30 years old and seemed to be from the lower class. After entering Room No. 2, they asked the waiter to bring a teapot and then talked in the room. Unexpectedly, less than a dozen minutes later, four thugs suddenly broke into the hotel. The thugs were all wearing black silk shirts and pants, looking very fierce.

Open Fire on Guests with Handguns: At the time, the hotel owner, Huang Jimei, was cooling off at the entrance. Seeing that the thugs looked suspicious, he was about to ask questions when one of the thugs stepped forward to stop him, monitored him, and said there was no need to announce the revenge, and there was no need to panic. As he spoke, three of them took out handguns from their sleeves and walked towards Room No. 2. Then, a series of gunshots, sounding like machine guns, were heard in the room for about a dozen times.

Great Bloodshed, Two Dead and Two Injured: The travelers and waiters in the hotel were shocked upon hearing the gunshots and hid in fear, not daring to investigate. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, the thugs walked out and fled without a trace. Afterwards, the hotel owner urgently sent someone to report the case to the Dadazimingzhong Police Station, who immediately sent Chinese and Western detectives to the scene to investigate and arrest the perpetrators. Blood was found all over the room. Two people had died from gunshot wounds, and two others were seriously injured, moaning in pain.

Sent to Hospital to Arrest Perpetrators: The two injured men were sent to Renji Hospital for treatment in a police car. One of them, wearing a willow shirt and pants, identified himself as Chen Yiming, from Yancheng, 34 years old, living near the West Gate. He stated that the perpetrators were all acquaintances, but he did not want to disclose the reason. He was shot twice, once in the right chest and once in the left foot. After being injured, he used both hands to hold down the wound and escaped from Room No. 2 to the lobby, where he collapsed on a rattan chair. The other injured man, wearing yellow shorts and a collared shirt, identified himself as Zhong Ziqing, 41 years old, from Jiangbei. His teacher, Ge, knew the details of his matter. He said that he was shot twice, once in the neck and once in the right hand. Both were in critical condition. After questioning the two, the police detectives went out to arrest the perpetrators.

Two Corpses Sent for Examination: The two corpses were sent to the morgue for examination by the court. The two deceased were both around 30 years old, one wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, and the other wearing a white undershirt and pants. The former was injured in the chest and foot, and the latter was injured in the brain and waist. One of them was the first to check into Room No. 2 of the "Fa Shang Hotel." The hotel owner, Huang Jimei, and the waiters were summoned by the police to inquire about the circumstances of the incident for verification.

Private Arms Trafficking Case

Additional Charge of Fraud 136

Bi Ke and Le Weisi Gai

Both charged with attempted blackmail and fraud

Wei Xiaolan accused of assisting in fraud

Le Weisi Gai presents a gas mask

Russian Bi Ke and Le Weisi Gai, colluded to impersonate officials of the National Government, ordered military supplies worth 1.8 million from Lai Fa, the owner of the British firm Lai Fa Yanghang on Guangdong Road, and forged Lai Fa's seal. After investigation by the police, a lawsuit was filed in the First Special District Court. After several interrogations, just as the case was about to conclude, Chief Inspector Hua Tan Ma Wenda and West Inspector Bei Zhining from the General Inspectorate arrested Wei Xiaolan at 33 Bushi Road in the French Concession. It was discovered that Wei had been associating with Le Weisi Gai and others at Lai Fa's place. Le pointed out that Wei was the secretary of Zhang Faying, a representative of the National Government. She was handed over to the Special Court for interrogation. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Jiashi of the Criminal Court continued the trial in Criminal Division One. The details are as follows:

The Customs' Response After the trial began yesterday, the police were represented by Lawyer Ru Bao Yi. Bi Ke and Le Weisi Gai were represented by Lawyer Yan Biao Fenling. Wei Xiaolan was represented by Lawyer Fan Gang, and translator Jiang Baoliang was appointed for this case. Lawyer Ru Bao Yi started by stating that the police are now additionally charging Bi Ke and Le Weisi Dong with attempted blackmail and fraud under Article 370, Section 3 of the Criminal Code, and Wei Xiaolan with assisting in the same. Judge Xu then instructed translator Jiang Baoliang to translate to Bi Ke, "This court has now received a letter from the Jianghai Customs Superintendent, stating that you once reported to the Customs that Lai Fa was privately selling military supplies to Guangdong. Later, a woman sent the contract, and she was not under the mission of Customs investigation, etc." Bi replied in the affirmative.

Zhang Faying's Secretary Judge Xu then turned to ask Wei Xiaolan whether she and Le Weisi Gai went to Le's house at 24 Shengmu Yuan Road through the introduction of a certain person named Xue Ge Lai Lai. She replied, "Yes. When I arrived at Le's house, Bi Ke also came in less than five minutes. He then asked me to go to Lai Fa's place, but Bi Ke did not go. When we arrived at the entrance of Lai Fa's place, I asked Le what he wanted me to say. He replied to listen to his command. Then we entered together. Le pointed to me and said to Lai Fa, 'This is the secretary of General Zhang Faying.' I did not say anything. Then they began to negotiate about military supplies." Judge Xu asked, "Who wanted to buy the military supplies?" She replied, "They were purchased by Guangdong." He asked, "Where were they being transported to?" She replied, "To Guangdong." He asked, "Who is the general?" She replied, "Zhang Faying is the brother of Zhang Fakui. This happened on May 24th."

Second Contact Judge Xu asked, "When was the second contact?" She replied, "About the next day. I immediately scolded Le, saying that I didn't want to be asked to do such illegal things again." He asked, "Was there any talk about who needed to prove or guarantee it the first time?" She replied, "No, it was only mentioned the next day. On the 25th, Bi Ke and Le Weisi Gai came to my house again and asked me to go to Lai Fa's place with them. I didn't want to. Le said that Lai Fa had prepared wine and dishes, so why not go? I was forced and had to go." He asked, "Did Le Weisi Gai tell you that as long as Zhu Ziyao signed, you could hire a lawyer to claim a commission, which would be very beneficial to you? Is that correct?" She replied, "Yes. When I went to Lai Fa's place the second time, Le asked who would guarantee it. At that time, there were two small photos hanging in the room. Lai Fa immediately said that these two people, one named Tang Jingji and the other Gu Xinyi, were both his friends and could be guarantors. Le expressed unwillingness. At that time, I asked Lai Fa whether Tang Jingji had a steel factory in Yangshupu. Lai Fa replied yes. Then Lai Fa said to Le, 'How about Zhu Ziyao?' Le replied, 'Good. If Zhu cannot guarantee, he can also testify.'" He asked, "Was there any talk about commission at that time?" She replied, "No, this matter was probably discussed before or after."

Little Cantonese Went Along Judge Xu asked, "Is there such a person as Zhang Faying?" She replied, "It's fake." He asked, "How do you know it's fake?" She replied, "Because I didn't want to go to Lai Fa's place with Le Wei Gai, Le said that I couldn't assume the position of general and that he would find someone a little older and resembling a general to impersonate Zhang Faying. Later, a Russian named Si Tiegaofu asked me why I didn't want to do this again. I told him the situation. He immediately said that Le had found someone, that is, the Little Cantonese who lights my cigarettes, to go with him. Then I knew it was a complete fake."

Zhu Ziyao's Testimony Judge Xu then summoned Lai Fa to the case and asked if he knew Wei Xiaolan. He replied, "I know her." He asked, "According to them, this batch of military supplies was purchased by Guangdong." He replied, "No, they said it was ordered by the National Government." He asked, "Since the contract for the purchase of military supplies has already been signed, why is there another order form for more than 500,000 yuan of military supplies? What does that mean?" He replied, "I suppose it was forged to defraud me and Zhu Ziyao of money in order to achieve the purpose of fraud. I request a thorough investigation." Then Zhu Ziyao was summoned. He asked, "What was the purpose of the defendant appointing lawyers Shi Zhuoren and Hailisi to your place?" He replied, "To claim a commission." He asked, "How much money did they want?" He replied, "Nine yuan for each gun." He asked, "Did the two lawyers say that if you didn't pay the commission, they would report that you were guaranteeing the purchase of military supplies on behalf of Guangdong, etc.?" He replied, "They only said that this batch of military supplies was purchased by Guangdong, which was extremely dangerous, etc."

Presenting a Gas Mask Then, lawyer Shi presented evidence, stating that he was commissioned by Le to claim a commission from Zhu Ziyao, totaling more than 69,000 yuan. Judge Xu then asked Le Weisi Gai whether Wei Xiaolan's statement was correct. He replied, "I met Wei at Lai Fa's place. She specializes in introducing the purchase of military supplies to Lai Fa to supply bandits. One day, Lai Fa ordered me to send ten pistols and more than a thousand bullets to Wei's house in the French Concession. The next day, Wei sent over a thousand yuan, the price of the guns." At this point, the court stopped him and asked what he meant by forging an order form for more than 500,000 yuan of military supplies, and he should explain it clearly. Le replied that Lai Fa had sold a kind of gas mask, and he had obtained evidence documents for it. The mask is now at the lawyer's office. The defendant's lawyer presented a mask, which looked like a rope net, to the court. He also claimed that there were many photos and items that were the poisons sold by the plaintiff, with receipts signed by Supervisor Tang and photos taken. Later, because the items were returned, the receipts were also returned.

Three Witnesses Judge Xu then asked Le whether he forged this order form in order to prove that Lai Fa was selling poisons and to gain the trust of Supervisor Tang. Le replied vaguely. Lawyer Ru Bao Yi then stood up and asked Le Weisi Gai who introduced him to Wei Xiaolan. He replied that it was introduced by Lai Fa. Lawyer Ru then stated to the court that the police initially thought that Le would not deny the details provided by Wei Xiaolan. Now, unexpectedly, the opposite is true, so the police have to present witnesses to prove it. The witnesses they want to present are Xue Ge Lai Lai, the introducer of Wei Xiaolan, and Wei's wife, Ms. Ye, and Wei's housemate, Ms. Dong Zhou. They should be interrogated. Then Xue Ge Lai Lai testified that Le Weisi Gai and Wei Xiaolan's acquaintance was introduced by him. Then Dong Zhou, Wei Ye, testified successively that Bi Ke and Le Weisi Gai had been to Wei's house several times and quarreled with Wei once, and then they did not come again. By this time, it was past noon, and the witness testimony was completed. Judge Xu then announced that the case would be adjourned and the debate would begin at a later date.
