Municipal Government

Deadline for Banning Rental Temples 140

Drafting measures to ban rental temples

Gradual ban by lottery within two years

The Municipal Government previously believed that rental temples only have abbots and no religious buildings, which does not comply with the provisions of Article 1 of the Regulations on Temple Registration promulgated by the Ministry of Interior. Moreover, the city is prosperous and not a place for pure cultivation, and it is difficult to ensure that there is no abuse of collecting money. It was ordered to ban them within a time limit. Later, the Chinese Buddhist Association and others repeatedly sent letters requesting an extension of the ban. The Municipal Government, in order to show its understanding, approved them one after another. Recently, the Municipal Government believes that the ban on rental temples cannot be delayed any longer and will order the drafting of banning measures, aiming to ban them in four phases by lottery within two years. It is learned that the above-mentioned banning measures have been announced and implemented by the Municipal Government. The details are as follows:

Shanghai Municipal Measures for Banning Rental Temples 141

1. Temples mentioned in these measures refer to temples established by monks, nuns, Taoists, and female Taoists who have rented houses in this city. 2. Rental temples shall register with the Public Security Bureau within one month from August 15th, 1931. 3. Rental temples that have been registered will be issued a registration certificate by the Public Security Bureau, which should be displayed in a prominent place. 4. Rental temples shall submit a certificate fee of two yuan and affix stamps when applying for a registration certificate. 5. Rental temples will be closed in four phases from the date of expiration of the registration period, with one-fourth closed in each phase. The first phase is the end of March 1932, the second phase is the end of September 1932, the third phase is the end of March 1933, and the fourth phase is the end of September 1933. 6. The rental temples to be closed in the first, second, and third phases will be determined by lottery. One month in advance, the Public Security Bureau will publish a notice in the newspaper about the number of households to be drawn. The lottery will be held before the 20th of the month. The temples to be closed in the fourth phase will be announced one month in advance. 7. When the lottery is held, in addition to the Social Affairs Bureau sending personnel to participate, legally organized monk and Taoist groups in the city may also send representatives to observe. 8. Those who fail to register after the registration deadline or fail to close when the deadline is reached will be closed by the Public Security Bureau. 9. Once a rental temple is registered, it is not allowed to move, and from the date of registration, it is not allowed to rent a house to establish a temple. 10. Rental temples that have been registered and voluntarily close shall submit a registration certificate to the Public Security Bureau for verification and cancellation. 11. If a registered rental temple violates laws and regulations, spreads rumors to confuse the public, does not abide by monastic rules, or violates the provisions of Article 9, it will be closed immediately. 12. These measures will be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

Announcement from the Cholera Prevention Office 142

The Shanghai Temporary Cholera Prevention Office issued the third announcement yesterday, stating: (1) According to reports from the Shanghai Chinese Concession health authorities, although no cholera outbreaks have been found in their respective jurisdictions, preventive measures are still being implemented. Special attention is being paid to factories, slum areas, and places where filth and flies are concentrated. (2) Regarding Zhoupu Town, which is ten miles east of Zhoujiadu in Shanghai (direct train access), the investigation report by medical officers Sun Zhirong and Sun Jiaqi is as follows: (A) A limited cholera outbreak occurred three weeks ago, with a total of 18 confirmed cases and five deaths. Their ages ranged from 5 to 66 years old. Those who recovered were due to saline injections. None of the above patients had received cholera vaccinations. (B) The residences of the above patients are all within a one-acre area northeast and south of Zhoupu. (C) Zhoupu is a lively town with a large match factory employing 700 workers. Four of the workers died of cholera this time. (D) The cause of infection for these patients does not seem to be due to the water supply. According to the investigation, it is actually due to flies spreading the cholera bacteria from the patients' feces. Our preventive work is focused on cleaning and disinfecting the town's toilets and preventing flies from coming into contact with them. (E) As of today, 6,700 people have been vaccinated against cholera. The cholera vaccination team sent by the health authorities patrols back and forth on the railway every day, eight times a day, administering vaccinations to passengers arriving in Shanghai from the epidemic area without exception. (F) In summary, the epidemic can be said to have been brought under control, as there have been no further cholera cases at the railway stations along the line. (3) Mr. Sheng Hou, a senior medical officer from the Tokyo Ministry of Interior's Disease Prevention Department, came to Shanghai for ten days (August 1st to August 11th) to investigate the city's health conditions. In the conversation, he said that the Japanese government greatly praised the quarantine work at this port. The Japanese government has now reinstated the Shanghai port and no longer appoints medical officers. Last year, there were a total of 127 cholera cases in Shanghai, and none of the Japanese ports declared Shanghai as an epidemic area. The cholera did not spread to Japan. (4) The cholera vaccination for passengers on the Ninglai ship is still carried out at around 3-4 am every morning when passing Wusong. From August 6th to 14th, a total of 6,730 passengers were vaccinated. Since August 2nd, a total of 10,810 people have been vaccinated. Wu Liande, Director of the National Seaport Quarantine Office.

The coastal residents were unable to sleep peacefully. A few days ago, Zheng went to Shanghai to add military supplies. The Changshu County Public Security Bureau stationed in Shanghai detected this and joined the Chinese and Western detectives of the Huisi Police Station (formerly the Xinzha Police Station by mistake) to arrest Zheng, searching out 2 Browning pistols. He was handed over to the Special District Court for questioning and ordered to be handed over to the Changshu County Government for interrogation and trial. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. It is learned that Yin Peng, the director of the Changshu County Public Security Bureau, believed that Zheng was a well-known pirate commander with many followers, and fearing negligence, he personally led eight box-gun squads and detectives to Shanghai the day before yesterday. He submitted a document requesting permission to extradite him. Director Yin then escorted Zheng on the Beijing-Shanghai train to Kunshan, transferred to a small boat, and escorted him back to Changshu for interrogation and trial.

Deserter Jumps from Train Window 152

Yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway's train number 32, a special express from Beijing Gate, departed from the North Station to Hangzhou. A deserter named Li Jinyong from the 1st Company, 2nd Platoon of the Artillery Battalion of the 4th Division of the Army stationed in Hangzhou, was being escorted by squad leader Chang Hua and Sun Liang from his company headquarters to Hangzhou for interrogation. Unexpectedly, as the train was departing from the Xinlonghua Station, the deserter Li Jinyong suddenly jumped out of the train window in an attempt to escape. The train could not stop at that time, so the escorting squad leader had to wait until the train reached Songjiang, get off the train, and pursue him along the way. However, he was unable to find him even late into the night and had to report it to his superiors for investigation.

Yesterday's Reception for All Circles Regarding the Exhibition 155

Exterior: Transportation and security are closely related

Wang: A special exhibition is held to inform the public

Yan: Hoping to drive cars all over China

Shuo: Striving is not in vain, even in death

The National Road Association, in order to make the people understand the importance of transportation, held a road exhibition in Shanghai. It is heard that the opening ceremony is scheduled for September 12th on Betang Road in the French Concession. To arouse the attention of all circles and strive for cooperation to promote the progress of the road market, a banquet was held yesterday at noon at the Lianhua General Assembly to entertain Western businessmen in the city. Those present included Minister Wang, Minister Kong (represented by Xu Jianping), American Commercial Counselor Arnold, American Commercial Officer Shi Fangnan, Road Exhibition Chairman Cao Yunxiang, Director-General Yang Nianzu, Chinese and Western Executive Directors Zheng Xitao and Jin Shibo, and foreign merchants Ford, Xiang Mao, China, Yad, and Fada Automobile Companies, as well as Tianxiang, Mobil, Asia, Jardine Matheson, Xinchang, and Huayang Companies. Minister Wang first gave a speech, emphasizing the importance of this exhibition and hoping that manufacturers would actively participate and promote ticket sales. The American Consul and the President of the British Chamber of Commerce and Exhibition Chairman Cao gave speeches, promoting road construction and the importance of joining the exhibition. Around 2:00 PM, a group photo was taken, and the meeting adjourned.

Then, at 3:00 PM, a tea party was held at the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to entertain Shanghai groups and leaders from all walks of life, as well as members of the association. Those present included Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, Industry Minister representative Xu Jianping, Deputy Minister Zhao Jinqing, Pacification Commissioner Zhang Zhijiang (newly elected Vice President of the Road Association), Lin Kanghou, Zhang Zhilian, Zhu Shaoping, Shen Yi, Xiang Kangyuan, Tang Jingxian, Wang Yingbin, Tao Guilin, Li Songquan, Dong XianGuang, Hua LaiFeng (representative of Guizhou Province), Wu Yunzhai, Tao Leqin, Li Shilin (engineer of the association), Director-General Wu Shan, Li Bake, Wu Dongchu, Zheng Zhengqiu, and foreign guests Mr. Louier, Norman, Halcand, L, M, Smith, Miss Viola Smith, Miss E. Hinder and Thedore Chen and S.C. Kingshung, Chinese & Foreign Executive Secutanes, etc. First, Minister Wang delivered the opening speech, briefly saying that ten years ago, China had only a few hundred miles of highways, and now it has reached 40,000 to 50,000 miles. This achievement is due to the support of the central government, provincial governments, and local governments, as well as the promotion by the people. Now, in order to make the people understand the importance of national transportation and security and commercial relations, a special exhibition is held to further promote the progress of the road market. More than 20 provinces across the country have sent representatives to participate, as far as Guizhou, which also specially sent Mr. Hua Laifeng to Shanghai to attend. In addition, governments and groups from various countries have also sent exhibits for display, some of which have already been received, and some are still on the way, which is of great benefit to promoting roads. Because of the vastness of China's land, convenient transportation is the top priority. If railways are built in the shortest possible time, it will not only require a lot of money, but also be too slow to solve the urgent need and is not suitable for long distances. As for roads, it is not the same. The completion of a road is fast and quick. Even if it is as short as 50 or 100 miles, it can be built independently. At present, the most difficult thing for roads in China is Weihaiwei. Since the reception commissioner Xu Zushan took office, he has paid attention to the construction of roads, advocating government and people to cooperate in using farmers' supply of equipment and materials, and the government has also worked hard. Therefore, all villages in Weihaiwei have roads, which are connected and convenient for travel, and the local atmosphere is booming and becoming more prosperous. Therefore, the association hopes that the people in various places will follow the example of Weihaiwei, so that road construction can make great progress. According to the current exhibition, there are two methods that can help each other: (1) renting booths to display products, and (2) promoting ticket sales. I believe that the late Premier attached great importance to material construction, and reforming China's roads is also one of the main policies of the Premier's Outline of National Construction. The construction of roads can be seen as early as possible, and politics, education, and economy can also be implemented and improved in turn, and gradually become better. If traffic is blocked, industry will not prosper, and if there is a bandit police, it will be inconvenient to transport troops. Therefore, the quality of the road association's management has a great relationship with the future governance of China. My wish is to be able to drive a car all over the 28 provinces of China, so it is not in vain to work hard to promote it, and I will be content even in death. Then Wu Shan reported on the achievements of the Road Association and the enthusiasm of all parties to participate in this exhibition. Lin Kanghou then gave a speech, saying that all things in China are not on track because there is no road. If you want everything to be on track, you must promote road construction. Therefore, as the saying goes, "If this road is not passable, if the road is passable, everything can be solved easily." Next, Zhang Zhijiang gave a speech, saying that the association did not abandon the humble and newly elected him as the vice president. He said that he could only follow behind everyone to promote the construction. The Premier's National Construction Strategy says that clothing, food, housing, and transportation are the essential elements of life, and transportation has a significant impact on inland security and national border defense. The brothers used to be in the northwest Mongolia and other places. They did not have much road traffic and had a very deep impression. Therefore, they felt that actively building roads was an urgent matter. Finally, tea and snacks were served, and a group photo was taken to dismiss the meeting.

French Mail Ship and Japanese Ship

Collided in the Huangpu River Yesterday 159

Both Suffered Heavy Losses

Yesterday morning, a collision occurred in the Huangpu River between a French mail ship and a Japanese freighter, causing heavy losses to both sides. After detailed investigation by reporters from all sides, the damage is recorded as follows:

Condition of the Collision: The French Mail Ship Company's Ong Gance, at 10:20 am yesterday morning, completed loading cargo and passengers at the China Merchants Bureau Middle Dock in Hongkou. When it set sail to exit the port, it ordered the Wudefeng tugboat to take it out to Wusong. At the beginning of sailing from the dock, the tugboat was backing up to the center of the river, and then turned east to throw anchor at the 1st and 2nd river cylinders in front of the Yesong Shipyard. The Kawasaki Steamship Company freighter Boutuson Maru, Bordeaux Moru, managed by Showa Corporation in Shanghai, was transporting goods from San Francisco, USA, to Shanghai, and was unloading goods at the river cylinder. Unexpectedly, the French mail ship had not yet turned straight, and was hit by the fierce tide, which was unstoppable. The bow of the French mail ship crashed into the bow of the Japanese ship. With a loud bang, both ships were damaged.

Both Bows Suffered Huge Damage: The Japanese ship was parked on the river cylinder. When the French mail ship collided with it, it was unable to back up and had to listen to the collision. The place where the Japanese ship was hit was the front of the bow. The French ship has 15,000 tons, and because of the huge tide, the bow was hit and the iron plate was torn down, the bow was damaged, and it was broken towards the sky. At a glance, it looked like a headless ship. The French mail ship was also hit back, and the left side of the bow was also broken due to excessive impact, and the outer iron plate was broken, creating a large hole. Fortunately, it was above the waterline, so it was not flooded, but the loss was also huge.

Personnel Sent to Investigate Damage: After the incident, the Japanese ship reported to Showa Yanghang and notified the French Mail Ship Company, and reported to the director of the Customs and Port Affairs Bureau. Each company sent a fair person to the ship to investigate the damage to the two ships and inquire about the truth of the accident. The issue of responsibility will be negotiated separately. The French mail ship could not miss the deadline, so it immediately set sail to exit the port. The damaged hole had to be repaired along the way, and then it would be sent to the factory after arriving in France. The bow of the Japanese ship has been smashed and needs to be overhauled in Shanghai. Yesterday, the goods were rushed to unload. After clearing the cabin, it will be sent to the dock. It is said that the loss of the two ships this time will be tens of thousands of yuan.

Special News from the Shipping Industry 160

Cancellation of Ship Certificates: The Shanghai shipping industry requested the Ministry to cancel the inner port ship certificates, which hinder business. The Ministry of Finance has approved it, and even the Yangtze River ship certificates have been abolished. However, the supplementary measures after the cancellation have been ordered by the Ministry of Communications to the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau to discuss with the customs and various shipping companies to come up with a proper plan. The results of the discussion are: (1) River boat licenses, except for foreign merchant boats, are allowed to be cancelled; (2) After the cancellation of the inner port boat licenses, there are concerns about tax evasion, and other methods should be discussed. It has been decided that if merchant ships travel to the inner port, they must fill out a request to send to customs, along with the ministry certificate, and hand it over to the ship for safekeeping. When the ship returns to the due date, the request form will be submitted to the customs for cancellation.

Dayu Sets Sail: Dalian Company's Daji ship has been completed since its reconstruction and renamed Dayu. It has resumed navigation to Tongyang yesterday. This ship has been greatly renovated, and the layout of the passenger seats is very spacious and beautiful, and it has hot and cold steam equipment. It is the most outstanding ship in the Tongyang line.

Anhui Wharf Submerged: Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received a telegram from Anqing, saying that due to the influence of the sharp increase in upstream water in central Anhui, the river water has been increasing day and night, and has submerged the land. The wharves of various shipping companies along the river have all entered the water, and the lower floors of the warehouses have been completely submerged in the water, and passengers cannot load or unload. Please Shanghai stop loading Anqing goods as soon as possible. Various circles are currently rescuing them.

The City Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Industries

National Goods Prices Must Not Be Raised 162

The City Chamber of Commerce yesterday issued a notice to all industry associations regarding the fact that national goods prices must not be raised during the period of boycott of Japanese goods: Dear Sirs, we have received a letter from the Secretariat of the Shanghai Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, No. 2883, which states that the third district party department reported that during this time of economic severance with Japan, it is an opportunity for national goods to sell well. All national goods factories and shops, in order to promote national goods and boycott Japanese goods, should sell national goods at fair prices, and at the same time, strive to improve the quality of national goods, so that the people of the whole country are happy to purchase them. However, it is reported that some unscrupulous merchants are madly raising the prices of national goods in secret, which has a great impact on the future of boycotting Japanese goods and promoting national goods. Please inform and advise all national goods shops not to raise the prices of national goods for no reason, so as to promote and benefit the boycott of Japanese goods. Based on this, the standing committee approved the transfer of the letter to the City Chamber of Commerce for handling. Correspondingly, the letter is sent to you for your reference and implementation. It is important to note that this is a good opportunity to develop national goods during the period of boycott of Japanese goods, and sales should be made at the same price to show promotion. Unfortunately, there are always short-sighted merchants who secretly raise prices and profit from them, which has a profound impact on the future of boycotting Japanese goods and promoting national goods. Now, in accordance with the previous reason, a corresponding letter is sent to you for your reference and transmission, and it is hoped that you will strictly abide by it.

Western Cuisine Industry

Workers Failed to Resume Work Yesterday 164

The Union Will Discuss the Report to the Authorities for Approval Today

After the workers in the Western cuisine industry in the city went on strike, they all complied with the order to resume work yesterday. Regarding the treatment conditions, they planned to wait quietly for the competent authorities to resolve them according to law. Unexpectedly, the management refused, so the resumption of work failed. The union has decided to hold a general meeting of members today to discuss countermeasures. The situation yesterday is recorded as follows:

Authorities Stop It: In addition to mediating the treatment conditions in the Western cuisine industry, the Social Bureau also approved the order of the Western Cuisine Industry Union to stop the strike: The report is noted. The union's request for the management to improve treatment should be submitted to the Bureau for approval in accordance with legal procedures. Automatic strike is very inappropriate. You are now required to instruct all workers to resume work on the 15th, and no mistakes are allowed. The order is urgent, and the industry association is ordered not to deliberately make things difficult when the workers resume work.

Refuse to Resume Work: The workers in the Western cuisine industry, in compliance with the order, went to resume work yesterday morning, accompanied by members of the union. Regarding the treatment conditions, they quietly waited for the Social Bureau to mediate according to law. Quan Jiafu, Pacific, Royal Palace, Zui Hechun, Yizhi Xiang, Daguanlou, Yijia Chun, Hengsheng, Jinlong, and other Western cuisine industry management all refused to resume work because they had already hired non-union members to work. All the workers had no choice but to withdraw and report to the union to be submitted to the party and government organs for handling.

Union Attitude: Yao Pingqing, standing director of the Western Cuisine Industry Union, told reporters from the New Sound Society that the workers' automatic strike was caused by the management's lack of sincerity in accepting the conditions, and the responsibility lies with the management. Today, all the workers are resuming work in compliance with the order, but the management actually refused. Moreover, the Social Bureau had previously ordered the management industry association not to deliberately make things difficult when the workers resumed work, so the management's violation of the law and the destruction of the labor movement have become obvious. The workers of this union were very angry, and fortunately, the union tried its best to dissuade them, so that no changes occurred. The union has now submitted the situation of the management refusing to resume work to the authorities for review, and requested that the treatment conditions be mediated as soon as possible.

Association's Statement: Reporters from the Wuchen Society yesterday ordered members of the Western Cuisine Industry Association Lin Zhenchuan and Yan Furen. The talks between the two gentlemen are recorded as follows: The two gentlemen said that the workers' strike was really unfortunate for the industry, and the operating losses have already been considerable. The treatment of workers in the industry has been very generous for decades. In addition to the wages they receive, the workers are given a dividend based on the business calculations, so they have been at peace for a long time. The proposed improvement of treatment conditions this time is a purely unreasonable demand, and it can be seen that they have been incited. Please explain: (1) The public account of small accounts is a long-standing custom in the industry. The small account is the dividend, which is calculated based on the total amount of business. Although the associate is the agent of the employer, he has personally entertained guests and responded to them in fact, so the small account he gets in return is not as much as they say, exceeding more than three shares. As for the miscellaneous expenses, it is actually the cost of the consumers of the guests who have obtained the dividend, such as towels, perfume, soap, and small items. Occasionally, they are compensated for it, and the amount is very small, and of course the shop owner cannot be asked to bear it. It is unprecedented to create a new name for it. (2) Extra rewards are small accounts given by customers after paying the bill, and are distributed to the workers who should serve and serve, and those who are not worth it are difficult to share. Both of these are true situations, and there have been examples of such things long before the workers requested improvement. As for articles (3) (5) (6), the conditions proposed are contrary to laws and regulations, and will not be discussed here. The fourth article, the so-called calculation of wages for double work in July and August of the lunar calendar, shows that among the businesses of the shops in the industry, only the business in July and August is relatively considerable, and the losses in the other ten months are inevitable. Therefore, the shops in the industry have losses every year, and they are almost unsustainable. As for Article (7), the kitchen leftovers, that is, fish heads and leftover tails, are related to the shop owner's capital, and are usually included in the small account and distributed publicly, and the benefits should be treated the same as the shop owner. Why bother to change things? The losses suffered by the shops in the industry due to the strike are really considerable. In order to maintain business and protect the city's peace, they have to hire other partners to work. It has been declared that the striking workers have been dismissed and reported to the City Social Bureau for record. It seems that the union's free action violates laws and regulations, causing unexpected losses to the industry. The late Premier once said, "Chinese workers are not yet oppressed by domestic capitalists. Since the labor tide, Chinese workers are not only not oppressed by domestic capitalists, but also want to use various methods to oppress domestic capitalists." Why can the industry be called capitalists? It is not easy to operate on a small scale, and how can it be destroyed? In order to respect laws and regulations and seek social security, the authorities should sanction them according to law.

The Case of the Collision of the New Kang Vessel Opened Yesterday 167

Defendant Japanese Post Office Did Not Attend

Litigation Assistance Provides Guarantee

The case of the China Merchants Bureau's New Kang vessel being sunk by the Japanese merchant Ryuno Maru two years ago, in which 205 family members of the victims, such as Gao Decai and Zhu Xiaoyun, sued the Japan Mail Steamship Company for damages of 1,101,861 yuan, 2 jiao and 7 fen, was heard in the 9th court of the Shanghai Special Zone Court yesterday morning by Judge Li Mo. No one from the defendant's side attended. The plaintiff was represented by lawyers Wu Jingxiong and Sheng Zhenwei. A large number of family members and groups attended the court to listen. First, Lawyer Sheng made a statement, and then he summoned the plaintiffs such as Zhu Xiaoyun for questioning. Regarding the issue of litigation fees, the plaintiff and the agent lawyer stated that since the unfortunate death of the family members of the victims, the lives of the family members of the victims were almost desperate. Those who were rescued were completely washed away with their property and were spared only with their lives. Now, most of them are unemployed and have no means of support, and it is still difficult to maintain their daily lives. They really have no energy to raise litigation fees. They requested to take into account the circumstances and allow litigation assistance. The judge then declared that the nature of this case is not comparable to ordinary civil cases. Although the Sino-Japanese treaty has expired and is invalid, there are actually many problems. Assistance can be approved, but a proper guarantee must be provided to prove that the family members of the victims are indeed unable to pay the litigation fees, in whole or in part. When the family members of the victims are ordered to bear the burden, they must guarantee that they will find ways to pay. The plaintiff and the agent lawyer promised to comply with the instructions and proceed. At this point, the court was adjourned and a date was set for another trial. It is heard that the family members of the victims plan to ask Yu Qiaqing, chairman of the Shanghai Shipping Association, to guarantee everything.

Selling Reactionary Newspapers 173

Fined Eighty Yuan

He was discovered by detectives from the Public Security Bureau. Because he violated the ban, he was arrested and taken to the police station along with the newspapers. After being reviewed by the Second Special Court, he was instructed to wait for a change of date for further interrogation. Yesterday was the date for the continued interrogation. He was sent to the Criminal Simple Court. First, the lawyer of the police station, Fei Xizhen, explained the case, and stated that the newspapers violated Articles 3, 19, and 35 of the Publishing Law and the French Consul's regulations on banning publications. He asked for an investigation. In He Jinzhi's confession, he said that a friend surnamed Zhao gave him the newspapers to sell. He did not know his address. He was uneducated, which led him to be fooled. He asked for leniency. After the judge Wu Fanglian verified the confession, he announced the end of the debate in court and sentenced the defendant to a fine of 80 yuan. If he was unable to pay, two yuan would be deducted for one day of imprisonment.

Ren Zhennan's Lawyer's License Revoked 174

Already Left Shanghai for Guangdong

Ren Zhennan, a lawyer of Guangdong origin, was accused of defrauding Yongshang Zhuang Chunfu of thousands of silver dollars in the Shanghai Local Court Procuratorate. The public prosecution has already been filed, and the court has ruled that Ren be released on bail pending trial. Ren's wife, Jiang, also filed a lawsuit in the Local Court Procuratorate accusing her husband of insulting women. Initially, the prosecution was dropped. Jiang refused to accept and petitioned the High Court for reconsideration. The High Court Procuratorate has now filed a public prosecution. The Shanghai Bar Association also believes that it is related to the ethics of the lawyers. It has now been decided to order Ren to withdraw from the association and submit it for disciplinary action. Ren has suffered such blows from several sides. He has already left Shanghai for Guangdong. His lawyer's license has been revoked by himself.

Free Talk

World Snippets 184

—Hai Ke

Throwing Shoes After the Wedding Ceremony

After European and American men and women have gone through the wedding ceremony, when they get in the car to go on their honeymoon, their relatives and friends often throw many old shoes at them. This is a common custom, and everyone is used to it. According to most people, its origin is very ancient. It was first created in Egypt. At that time, there were many races who regarded women as a kind of property. The Jews were especially like this. When trading with people, they would hand over a shoe as a settlement. When women married, it was like a kind of transaction, so shoes were also used. Down to the present, it has become a custom of throwing shoes through miscommunication.

Others say that among savage races, the custom of kidnapping brides was prevalent. The groom often rode alone to the bride's home and kidnapped the bride alive. His family was unwilling to give up and came out to chase him. Unable to catch up, they had to throw things up in the back to vent their anger. Unexpectedly, this savage custom has now been adopted by civilized people.

An old custom of the Saxons: When a woman got married, her father always had to give one of her shoes to the groom. The groom took it in his hand and touched it on the bride's forehead to show that he could discipline her in the future. This is also a legacy of ancient times, and in modern times, it has been unknowingly entangled.

Record of the Ceremony for Awarding Certificates of the Higher Examination 185

—Jie Shan

Ninety-nine people, including Zhu Leizhang, passed the five examinations of this year's Higher Examination. The ceremony for awarding the passing certificates was held in the auditorium of the Examination Yuan at 8:00 AM on the 12th. Central Committee members and heads of various ministries were present, including Chen Bulei, Liu Ruiheng, Ma Fuxiang, Ru Yuli, Chen Yi, and Miao Fucheng. Dai Chuanxian, the president of the Examination Yuan, Shao Yuanchong, the chairman of the Examination Committee, Wang Yongbin, the vice chairman, and all the associate examiners, examiners, supervisors, and committee members, as well as hundreds of officials above the rank of Jianren in the Examination Yuan and its affiliated ministries. Eighty-seven of the passers were present. There were many things to see and hear during the ceremony. I will describe them as follows.

The situation of awarding certificates When awarding certificates, Dai Chuanxian and the chairmen of the Examination Committee, Shao Yuanchong and Wang Yongbin, personally awarded the certificates by name. The candidates stood in a row in solemn silence. When their name was called, they responded and went three steps forward to the front of the podium. They stood upright and bowed to the certificate presenter. They stepped forward three steps and respectfully received the certificate with both hands. Then, they stepped back three steps to their original position and stood upright. They held the certificate in their left hand, let their right hand hang down, and bowed to the certificate presenter. After the ceremony, they slowly returned to the row. All the candidates were respectful and respectful when receiving the certificate, and it was quite quiet.

Speeches and Replies After the certificates were awarded, Central Committee member Chen Bulei gave a speech first, followed by National Government member Liu Ruiheng. Then, President Dai and Chairman Shao gave speeches. The words were all encouraging and inspiring, and the expectations for the candidates were very high. After the speeches, Zhou Bangdao, who was publicly recommended by the candidates as the first-class candidate for educational administration personnel, gave a reply. Mr. Zhou's words were solemn and slightly humorous, and the listeners were quite satisfied.

A glimpse of the prizes In addition to each member of the examination office receiving a silver commemorative badge as a souvenir, those who were listed as first-class were also given a complete set of the Prime Minister's works in a fine binding by President Dai and a copy of the Covenant printed by the National Assembly. Those who were excellent were given a complete set of the Prime Minister's works in a regular binding. Chairman Shao gave a complete set of the collected volumes of the Construction Monthly to the first and second place winners of each test. And a mirror frame written by himself. The inscriptions were: "Articles Illuminate the Country," "Heavy Responsibility and Distant Zhi," "Covering the Middle and Manifesting the Outer," "Great Virtue Carries Things," and "Healthy Action," etc.) In addition, Ms. Zhang Mojun, a member of the examination committee, was good at calligraphy and wrote five folding fans to give to the four who were listed as first-class. The remaining one was given to Xue Quanzeng, who passed two examinations at the same time. Shao also gave Mr. Xue a mirror frame and a copy of the Construction Monthly to show his excellence.

A banquet at Hualin Hall After the ceremony, a photo was taken and a visit to the mausoleum was made. At noon at 12 o'clock, the Examination Yuan hosted a banquet in the Hualin Hall of the Yuan (ie, the library of the Yuan) to entertain the candidates. Drinks were exchanged and the hosts and guests were happy. It was not until 3:00 PM that the event ended. The candidates left the door with a spring breeze on their faces. Their pride can be known. (Que Chou)

Coal-Made Protein 186

—Update

Professor Klent of Germany recently made a surprising report at the annual meeting of the Bochum Scientific Research Association, that is, a new discovery that protein can be extracted from coal. According to Dr. Klent, he has proven the relationship between a certain by-product of coal and animal protein. This new discovery is indeed very important. Because in terms of production value, coal-made protein is easier to compete with than animal products. Although it is not yet time to replace natural products with artificial products as food, it is quite possible to use mineral protein as food. It is also heard that this new discovery of Ke will be subjected to large-scale experiments to make it applicable and benefit the world.

Record of the Independence Parade in the Philippines 187

—Wen Chu sent from Manila

The enthusiasm of the Filipinos for independence can be said to be even greater. At present, the ruling tycoons and merchants in the business community have a perfunctory attitude. The United States wants to compete for naval power in the Pacific Ocean and cannot abandon its naval base in the East. And the major merchants do not want to import more than 150 million items of goods into the Philippines every year. Once they are subject to tariff restrictions with other countries. (Philippine customs revenue. The United States, as the sovereign state, has tax-free preferential rights. Therefore, American goods account for 65% of imports each year.) However, Philippine sugar exported to the United States also enjoys tax-free preferential rights. The southern provinces of the United States are sugar producing areas and are affected by competition in trade. Congressional representatives from the province strongly advocate allowing the Philippines to become independent immediately in order to avoid hindering American agriculture. This is why there are often human……justice……tones in Congress. It seems to be speaking out for the Filipinos.

US Senator Howe is the most supportive of Philippine independence. This time, he came to the Philippines to investigate the political and social conditions, as materials for discussion in the US Congress in the future. The Philippine legislature believes that the Filipinos should have a clear expression, so that Howe has a deep impression. Therefore, the independence parade was prepared on the previous Sunday to show that the Philippine people's demand for independence comes from the rational public opinion of the majority of the people.

All government personnel in Manila and nearby provinces, regardless of official rank, and registered social organizations and major factories, must join the parade. Railway companies offer special free tickets to on-the-job personnel and social organizations in various provinces. Therefore, on that day, train passengers were very crowded. Various social organizations also urged military bands to help the fun and join the number of people. There were more than 150,000 people. There was almost no space in front of the Congress and the large grass field for shade. Tram cars and horse-drawn carriages cut off traffic for almost three hours.

On that day, people from all walks of life, both men and women, wore a common uniform made from Philippine-produced and self-made materials. General Yaginado, the first republican president who abdicated 31 years ago, and Luo Xia, the current Speaker of the House, also held the independence flag and led the way in civilian uniforms. However, schools are bound by the established rules that they cannot join any political movement. Therefore, students from Chinese and major universities can only join the parade as individuals and cannot use the names of their respective schools.

Eulogy for Xu Qishang 188

—Ji Zhai

Qishang's name is Pengling, from Qingpu, Jiangsu. A Jinshi in the Gui Mao year, he was a director of the Ministry of Justice. He graduated from the Jinshi Hall and then graduated from the Faculty of Law of the Central University of Japan. He returned to China in the early years of the Republic of China and served as the director of the Criminal Division of the Ministry of Justice and the presiding judge of the Criminal Court of the Dali Yuan. He has written manuscripts such as Annotations on the Criminal Laws of Various Countries and Lectures on Criminal Procedure Law. Two years ago, the national capital moved south and he returned to his hometown to practice law. He lived in Zhang's Villa, Tong Deli, Xiaoyi Fang, Suzhou. He died of illness in late June. The poem recalls Jiangnan's regional examination in the Renyin year. There were four people from the same hometown in the same year. You mourn him.

He has the least talent and fame. I became closer because of the neighborhood. The Central Plains gave me a dream of the past. I followed the dust to see the sights of Beique. In the bleak and Xiao Xiao plum rain, the obituary came from Taihu Lake.

Last winter, I visited the old place in Suzhou. I only heard about the old age and sorrow. We met for a short time for half a year. Who knew that we would be separated forever. The fall of the legalist is not a private mourning. The remaining manuscripts should be searched as soon as possible. The testamentary book clarifies the science of criminal law. Dongying does not have to be inferior to Western Europe.

Travels in India (82) 189

—Linghua

On this day, I visited the small village north of the Deer Garden Sana University. The houses are low and small. It is still a yellow tile house. It is only separated by a river from the ruins of Sana. This river does not seem to be a long river. Or a large pond. Can't tell. There are several shepherdesses and cattle among them. Go to the village from here. There is no main road. There are few trees. And the road south of Sana. How neat it is. Like the road in the Shanghai Concession. The trees are also tall. The trees in the village are small and there are many cacti. There is wheat field next to it. Men and women are harvesting wheat. There is no rain in the dry season. A lot of dust. There are many white cows in the village. How dark the children are. I observe the darkness of the children. I know that it is indeed a racial relationship. Indians are very particular about bloodlines. Do not intermarry with other races. However, their appearance is not superior to other races. Only vegetarianism to connect with God. Indifferent and few desires. Although. Indians excel in the study of internal light. Children do not dislike their mothers ugly. Dogs don't dislike their families poor. Now all countries hold disciple rituals to worship the Buddha and Hinduism. Why should I use my naked eyes to look at the black people of India. Zhuangzi said. Tao gives it appearance. Heaven gives it form. Indians do not talk about industry and agriculture. The fields are not lush. The amount of harvest. Should not be good. Because they raise many cattle. So collect cow dung. And make it into cakes to burn it. It's all the same everywhere. Same as northern China. I often pass by various villages. Indian dogs do not seem to bite people very much. Or the countryside is all poor people. Belonging to the inferior ethnic group of the fourth level. There are only awe of the three tribes above.

I asked the Ceylonese master. Are there any surviving royal families of the Buddha today? The master replied no. A gentleman next to him said that the Shakya clan was hated by a certain king at that time. A certain king would destroy his clan. Asked how many people would be left if they were willing to keep their clan. Intermarriage is also possible. The Shakya clan replied that they did not want to stay. A certain king killed them all. I don't remember much. It seems like the affair of King Glazed Tile's attack on the Shakya clan. At that time, the Buddha was still alive. The Buddha originally viewed resentment and relatives as equal. The four great things are empty. There is no one in his descendants. It is not the Buddha's concern. I also asked if there were any surviving relatives of the Buddha's family. The person did not know either. For a long time, he said. The old capital of the Buddha, Kapilavastu, is now in ruins. If there are any survivors among his relatives, they may be in Nepal. The reason for the visit is that it is close to Nepal. I will use science to study according to the scriptures. Those who will reconcile the world's killing opportunities in the future are only in using the method of intermarriage. To greatly mix bloodlines. Try to view the extinction of the Shakya clan, which is not without the reason that it did not intermarry with other ethnic groups.

Rotary Club of Storytellers

Women, Women (21) 190

—Yao Su Feng

Let's leave the matter here for now. Let's just say that Xiao Rong's wife took a car to Tongfu Road. According to the number of the house that Mr. Li told her, she found Miss Ding's house.

She was very timid. At first, she really felt that she didn't have the courage to knock on the two doors. But later, she was burned by angry emotions and couldn't control herself after all. So she walked forward and knocked hard on the door.

Miss Ding happened to have returned from Suzhou. She had only been home for two hours. She was dozing upstairs. When she heard someone knocking on the door below, but not ringing the doorbell, she naturally felt very strange. She called Qiu Zi and asked her to see who was knocking on the door. Qiu Zi was in the room inside. At first, she didn't hear it. When Miss Ding called her, she quickly went downstairs to open the door.

Xiao Rong's wife originally came with a belly full of resentment, but she couldn't vent it when she saw people. When Qiu Zi opened the door, she was stunned and didn't know what to say.

"Who are you looking for?" Qiu Zi was very strange when she saw that the person knocking on the door was an unfamiliar woman.

"I'm here to look for Xiao Rong!" she said without thinking.

"Xiao Rong? There's no such person here! You're looking for the wrong person!"

"Then is this the Ding family?" Xiao Rong's wife was a little anxious.

"That's right!" Qiu Zi replied.

"Don't you have a lady who has been to Suzhou?"

"Yes! What are you asking him for?"

"I'm here to look for that person surnamed Lu who went to Suzhou with the lady here!"

"Ah! It's Mr. Lu! You didn't say so earlier! He's not called Xiao Rong! But what's the matter with you looking for him?" Qiu Zi was very suspicious.

Xiao Rong's wife saw that Qiu Zi was very kind. She only felt that she had no place to vent her full of resentment. Instead, she told her in a low voice: "He is my husband?......I have important things to say to him in person!"

Qiu Zi almost didn't believe it! She thought of Mr. Lu's appearance in her mind, and then looked at the woman in front of her who called Mr. Lu her husband. She felt confused and couldn't figure it out. She only said in surprise: "What? That Mr. Lu is your husband?"

"How can I make a confused and random identification? Just call him out!" Xiao Rong's wife suppressed her anger again and said with a pleading expression.

"Mr. Lu came and went out again! But wait for me to tell our lady! You wait, maybe our lady will see you." Qiu Zi was really smart. She immediately understood the importance of this matter.

On the one hand, Xiao Rong's wife could only wait outside the door. On the other hand, Qiu Zi flew upstairs to report.

Futures Gold Market Shows Tendency to Rise 192

The Bull Side Posts Three Taels Plus

Yesterday, the 15th, the gold exchange market began its forward transactions. Because today is Sunday, it was moved forward by one day. The market officially opened at 8 o'clock in the morning. However, gold firms arrived even earlier, gathering outside the exchange as early as 6 or 7 o'clock to start trading. The bull side was posting three taels and two or three qian for September to October, initially at three taels, with a listed price of three taels one qian five fen, later fluctuating around three taels. It is rumored that the bull and bear sides have not completely settled their transactions, with the bear side gaining momentum. Qian Changxiang, Chengfeng, Yongyongheng, and those hedging positions are mostly on the bull side. Yuanmaoyong, Dadecheng, Tongfeng, Henghengxing, and spot firms are all bears. It is expected that September will have no further significant activity, with most switching to October contracts. The opening price was 772 taels and 8 qian 5 fen, and the closing price was 75 taels and 5 fen, a rebound of 4 taels and 2 qian compared to the previous day. This is due to the conversion based on the listed price for October contracts. As for the October market, it seems to be trending upward, but the fluctuations are moderate. From morning to noon, it fluctuated by no more than six taels, and trading was slow. This is likely because the foreign exchange rate is stable, the silver market is inactive, and although U.S. stocks rose, there was no impact. The opening was high, but later, due to buyer activity, it briefly exceeded 780 taels before falling back, with only one or two taels of fluctuation. Finally, it was above 78 taels. The afternoon market was closed due to Saturday. It is recalled that the situation had been quite good this week, with the lowest price being 756 taels in the early morning of Monday, and the highest being 85 taels and a half the next day, a difference of 29 taels and 5 qian. Overall, September has seen a rise of about 24 taels, which is considered significant.

The opening price for October was 776 taels. Large silver bars showed no price changes. Private telegrams were at 1/16, so sentiment seemed good. Yarn and Cotton Yarn Market Shows Slight Improvement 197

The yarn market is slightly firmer, with a slight upward trend. However, it is difficult to be optimistic about the global cotton industry, and a small fluctuation may be necessary at present.

U.S. Cotton Destruction Plan Fails 200

Washington dispatch, 14th: The Department of Agriculture's plan to destroy one-third of the new cotton crop seems likely to fail because, according to unofficial indications, seven of the fourteen provinces do not approve, three provinces approve, and the remaining four provinces have not expressed an opinion.

U.S. Cotton Rises After Initial Drop Last Week 201

Cotton Production Destruction Plan Seems Difficult to Achieve

A telegram from New York on the 14th reported on the cotton market during the week: The government's cotton production estimate reached 15,584,000 bales, which was beyond the expectations of the public. As a result, everyone tended to sell, and the closing of bull positions was particularly strong. However, when prices fell, it attracted buying by the same industry and short covering, which may slightly prevent further market crashes. Afterward, market sentiment became more stable because market prices were actually too low, and the new crop was still not out of danger. In the current situation, with the new cotton production quantity added, the rollover number can reach at least 24,500,000 bales, so those who buy at higher values are undoubtedly timid. The public deeply believes that the new crop will progress smoothly this month. The Bureau of Agricultural Economics' proposal to destroy one-third of the cotton crop caused a temporary disturbance and enabled short covering. However, the industry is doubtful about the success of its plan. There is very little hedging in the South, and perhaps they will bear the burden of allocation before the new crop is harvested. Foreign Rice Continues to Fall 204

In addition to those already arriving, more will be arriving continuously. Those who set the price in other ports will also arrive. Moreover, after the recent frantic buying, appetites are also satisfied. Therefore, everyone's hearts are bearish, and they dare not handle too much. The actual retail sales on this street are also sluggish. Only those on this street who are thinking about doing business slightly handled it, and the price fell by another two jiao. Flour Market Ends Well 205

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month showed a trend of initial flatness followed by a beautiful appearance. The quotation for foreign wheat had decreased by about one or two jiao. However, most manufacturers' thoughts were that various places were suffering from floods, and the disaster situation was severe, so the attitude of the mainland groups was always very smooth in purchasing, so most were temporarily waiting and suspended sales. Recently, due to disaster relief sales, there was a slight increase, while the future was rarely moving. Due to the manufacturers' wait-and-see attitude, the market was active for those outside the industry, so each month was beautiful again. As a result, this month was up 1 fen and 2.5 li compared to the previous day, September was good by 1.5 fen, October was good by 1.75 li, November was good by 1.5 fen, December was good by 1.75 li, and January was good by 1.5 fen.

Both Futures and Spot Wheat Show Stable Trend 206

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month generally showed a firm and stable trend. Although the quotation for foreign wheat was still slightly lower, the foreign wheat in the hands of short accounts was inevitably unprofitable due to the continuous sharp decline, so they all tended to wait and see and were unwilling to easily sell. With the scarcity of sellers, buyers seemed to be firmer again, so the opening prices for each month were all stable and beautiful, improving by four or five fen compared to the previous day's closing price. There is no hope for over-涨 in the future because the source of foreign wheat has not been cut off after all. As a result, this month was better by 1 fen compared to the previous day, September was better by 4 fen, October was better by 5 fen, November and December were better by 4 fen. The spot wheat market situation still appears stable, with a low source of arrival and a thin bottom. However, the factory appetite is still dull, and more than 2,600 bags of Kai Shan, Shuangfeng, Fangtai, Haining, and Taicang wheat were handled by Fuxin Huafeng.

Silk and Tea New York Cantonese Silk Prices Still Weak 208

Exchange Rate Declines, Apparently Rising But Secretly Weak

The New York market's raw silk market has recently shown no sign of recovery. Japanese silk competition remains strong, and prices are becoming cheaper. Cantonese silk mills remain hesitant to purchase. Although prices rose on Wednesday, the exchange rate declined, resulting in an apparent rise but a hidden weakness. Fine grade Cantonese silk was quoted at $1.85 per pound, and coarse grade at $1.37 (US dollars). Transactions remain scarce, it is said.
